## 1. Configuração do Airbyte para Ingestão em Tempo Real

**/airbyte/connectors/streaming_source.py**
```python
import json
import time
from typing import Dict, Generator
from airbyte_cdk import AirbyteLogger
from airbyte_cdk.sources import Source
from airbyte_cdk.models import (
    AirbyteMessage,
    AirbyteRecordMessage,
    AirbyteStateMessage,
    AirbyteStream,
    ConfiguredAirbyteCatalog,
    ConfiguredAirbyteStream,
    SyncMode,
    Type,
)

class StreamingSource(Source):
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = AirbyteLogger()
        self.state = {}

    def check(self, logger: AirbyteLogger, config: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Validar configuração da fonte"""
        try:
            # Testar conexão com a fonte de streaming
            return {"status": "SUCCEEDED"}
        except Exception as e:
            return {"status": "FAILED", "message": str(e)}

    def discover(self, logger: AirbyteLogger, config: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Definir schema dos streams disponíveis"""
        streams = [
            AirbyteStream(
                name="events_stream",
                json_schema={
                    "type": "object",
                    "properties": {
                        "event_id": {"type": "string"},
                        "timestamp": {"type": "string", "format": "date-time"},
                        "user_id": {"type": "string"},
                        "event_type": {"type": "string"},
                        "properties": {"type": "object"},
                        "metadata": {"type": "object"}
                    }
                },
                supported_sync_modes=[SyncMode.full_refresh, SyncMode.incremental]
            ),
            AirbyteStream(
                name="llm_calls_stream",
                json_schema={
                    "type": "object",
                    "properties": {
                        "call_id": {"type": "string"},
                        "timestamp": {"type": "string", "format": "date-time"},
                        "model": {"type": "string"},
                        "tokens_input": {"type": "integer"},
                        "tokens_output": {"type": "integer"},
                        "latency_ms": {"type": "number"},
                        "feature": {"type": "string"}
                    }
                },
                supported_sync_modes=[SyncMode.full_refresh, SyncMode.incremental]
            )
        ]
        return {"streams": streams}

    def read(
        self,
        logger: AirbyteLogger,
        config: Dict,
        catalog: ConfiguredAirbyteCatalog,
        state: Dict = None
    ) -> Generator[AirbyteMessage, None, None]:
        """Ler dados em streaming da fonte"""
        if state:
            self.state = state

        # Simular conexão com fonte de streaming real (Kafka, Pub/Sub, etc)
        while True:
            try:
                # Em implementação real, substituir por conexão com fonte de streaming
                for stream in catalog.streams:
                    if stream.stream.name == "events_stream":
                        # Simular recebimento de eventos
                        record = {
                            "event_id": f"evt_{int(time.time())}_{hash(time.time())}",
                            "timestamp": time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ"),
                            "user_id": f"user_{hash(time.time()) % 1000}",
                            "event_type": "click" if hash(time.time()) % 2 == 0 else "view",
                            "properties": {"page": "home", "section": "hero"},
                            "metadata": {"ip": "192.168.1.1", "user_agent": "Mozilla"}
                        }
                        yield AirbyteMessage(
                            type=Type.RECORD,
                            record=AirbyteRecordMessage(
                                stream=stream.stream.name,
                                data=record,
                                emitted_at=int(time.time() * 1000)
                            )
                        )

                    elif stream.stream.name == "llm_calls_stream":
                        # Simular recebimento de chamadas LLM
                        record = {
                            "call_id": f"call_{int(time.time())}_{hash(time.time())}",
                            "timestamp": time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ"),
                            "model": "gpt-4" if hash(time.time()) % 2 == 0 else "gpt-3.5-turbo",
                            "tokens_input": hash(time.time()) % 1000,
                            "tokens_output": hash(time.time()) % 2000,
                            "latency_ms": hash(time.time()) % 500,
                            "feature": "chat" if hash(time.time()) % 2 == 0 else "search"
                        }
                        yield AirbyteMessage(
                            type=Type.RECORD,
                            record=AirbyteRecordMessage(
                                stream=stream.stream.name,
                                data=record,
                                emitted_at=int(time.time() * 1000)
                            )
                        )

                # Atualizar estado periodicamente
                self.state["last_emitted"] = int(time.time())
                yield AirbyteMessage(
                    type=Type.STATE,
                    state=AirbyteStateMessage(data=self.state)
                )

                time.sleep(1)  # Simular delay entre mensagens

            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Erro no streaming: {str(e)}")
                time.sleep(5)  # Aguardar antes de tentar novamente
```

## 2. Configuração do dbt com Modo Hive para Processamento Paralelo

**/dbt/dbt_project.yml**
```yaml
name: 'diyapp_evolution'
version: '12.0.0'
config-version: 2

profile: 'bigquery'

source-paths: ["models"]
analysis-paths: ["analysis"]
test-paths: ["tests"]
data-paths: ["data"]
macro-paths: ["macros"]
snapshot-paths: ["snapshots"]

target-path: "target"
clean-targets:
  - "target"
  - "dbt_packages"

models:
  diyapp_evolution:
    raw:
      +materialized: table
      +schema: raw
      +tags: ["raw"]
    staging:
      +materialized: incremental
      +schema: staging
      +tags: ["staging"]
      +incremental_strategy: merge
      +unique_key: id
    marts:
      +materialized: incremental
      +schema: marts
      +tags: ["marts"]
      +incremental_strategy: merge
      product:
        +schema: mart_product
      ai:
        +schema: mart_ai
      ops:
        +schema: mart_ops

vars:
  hive_mode_enabled: true
  realtime_window_minutes: 5
```

**/dbt/macros/hive_mode.sql**
```sql
{% macro enable_hive_mode() %}
  {# Macro para ativar o modo Hive no BigQuery para processamento paralelo #}
  {% if var('hive_mode_enabled', false) %}
    SET @@hive_partitioning_options = 'TRUE';
    SET @@hive_partition_pruning = 'TRUE';
    SET @@hive_partitioning = 'TRUE';
  {% endif %}
{% endmacro %}

{% macro get_realtime_window() %}
  {# Retorna a janela de tempo para processamento em tempo real #}
  {% set window_minutes = var('realtime_window_minutes', 5) %}
  {{ return(datetime.datetime.utcnow() - datetime.timedelta(minutes=window_minutes)) }}
{% endmacro %}
```

**/dbt/models/raw/raw_events.sql**
```sql
{{ config(
    materialized='table',
    schema='raw',
    tags=['raw']
) }}

-- Tabela raw para eventos em tempo real
SELECT
  event_id,
  timestamp,
  user_id,
  event_type,
  properties,
  metadata,
  _airbyte_emitted_at AS airbyte_emitted_at,
  _airbyte_ab_id AS airbyte_batch_id
FROM {{ source('airbyte', 'events_stream') }}

{% if is_incremental() %}
  -- Processamento incremental apenas para novos registros
  WHERE timestamp >= TIMESTAMP_SUB(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(), INTERVAL 1 HOUR)
{% endif %}
```

**/dbt/models/staging/stg_events.sql**
```sql
{{ config(
    materialized='incremental',
    schema='staging',
    tags=['staging'],
    incremental_strategy='merge',
    unique_key='event_id',
    partition_by={'field': 'event_date', 'data_type': 'date'}
) }}

{{ enable_hive_mode() }}

WITH raw_events AS (
  SELECT * FROM {{ ref('raw_events') }}
)

SELECT
  event_id,
  timestamp,
  DATE(timestamp) AS event_date,
  user_id,
  event_type,
  -- Parse do JSON properties
  JSON_VALUE(properties, '$.page') AS page,
  JSON_VALUE(properties, '$.section') AS section,
  -- Parse do JSON metadata
  JSON_VALUE(metadata, '$.ip') AS ip_address,
  JSON_VALUE(metadata, '$.user_agent') AS user_agent,
  -- Campos de controle
  airbyte_emitted_at,
  airbyte_batch_id,
  CURRENT_TIMESTAMP() AS processed_at
FROM raw_events

{% if is_incremental() %}
  -- Processamento incremental apenas para novos registros
  WHERE timestamp >= TIMESTAMP_SUB(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(), INTERVAL {{ var('realtime_window_minutes') }} MINUTE)
{% endif %}
```

**/dbt/models/marts/mart_product/realtime_metrics.sql**
```sql
{{ config(
    materialized='incremental',
    schema='mart_product',
    tags=['marts', 'product'],
    incremental_strategy='merge',
    unique_key='metric_key',
    partition_by={'field': 'metric_date', 'data_type': 'date'}
) }}

{{ enable_hive_mode() }}

WITH
-- Eventos do período
recent_events AS (
  SELECT
    event_id,
    timestamp,
    event_date,
    user_id,
    event_type,
    page,
    section
  FROM {{ ref('stg_events') }}
  WHERE timestamp >= {{ get_realtime_window() }}
),

-- Métricas por página
page_metrics AS (
  SELECT
    page,
    event_date AS metric_date,
    COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) AS unique_visitors,
    COUNT(*) AS total_events,
    COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN event_type = 'click' THEN user_id END) AS unique_clicks,
    COUNT(CASE WHEN event_type = 'click' THEN 1 END) AS total_clicks
  FROM recent_events
  GROUP BY page, event_date
),

-- Métricas por seção
section_metrics AS (
  SELECT
    section,
    event_date AS metric_date,
    COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) AS unique_visitors,
    COUNT(*) AS total_events
  FROM recent_events
  GROUP BY section, event_date
),

-- Métricas gerais
global_metrics AS (
  SELECT
    event_date AS metric_date,
    COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) AS dau,
    COUNT(*) AS total_events,
    COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN event_type = 'click' THEN user_id END) AS unique_click_users,
    COUNT(CASE WHEN event_type = 'click' THEN 1 END) AS total_clicks
  FROM recent_events
  GROUP BY event_date
)

-- Combinação de todas as métricas
SELECT
  CONCAT('page_', page) AS metric_key,
  metric_date,
  'page' AS metric_type,
  page AS dimension_value,
  unique_visitors,
  total_events,
  unique_clicks,
  total_clicks,
  CURRENT_TIMESTAMP() AS updated_at
FROM page_metrics

UNION ALL

SELECT
  CONCAT('section_', section) AS metric_key,
  metric_date,
  'section' AS metric_type,
  section AS dimension_value,
  unique_visitors,
  total_events,
  NULL AS unique_clicks,
  NULL AS total_clicks,
  CURRENT_TIMESTAMP() AS updated_at
FROM section_metrics

UNION ALL

SELECT
  'global' AS metric_key,
  metric_date,
  'global' AS metric_type,
  NULL AS dimension_value,
  dau AS unique_visitors,
  total_events,
  unique_click_users AS unique_clicks,
  total_clicks,
  CURRENT_TIMESTAMP() AS updated_at
FROM global_metrics

{% if is_incremental() %}
  -- Atualizar apenas métricas do período recente
  WHERE metric_date >= DATE_SUB(CURRENT_DATE(), INTERVAL 1 DAY)
{% endif %}
```

## 3. Orquestração com Prefect para Processamento Paralelo

**/prefect/flows/realtime_pipeline.py**
```python
import os
from datetime import timedelta
from prefect import flow, task, get_run_logger
from prefect.task_runners import ConcurrentTaskRunner
from prefect.artifacts import create_markdown_artifact
from prefect.blocks.notifications import SlackWebhook
from dbt.cli.main import dbtRunner
from google.cloud import bigquery
from google.api_core.exceptions import NotFound

# Configurações
DBT_PROJECT_DIR = "/opt/dbt/diyapp_evolution"
AIRBYTE_CONNECTION_ID = "streaming_connection"
SLACK_WEBHOOK_BLOCK = "slack-alerts"

@task(name="run_dbt_model", retries=2, retry_delay_seconds=30)
def run_dbt_model(model_name: str, full_refresh: bool = False):
    """Executa um modelo dbt específico"""
    logger = get_run_logger()
    logger.info(f"Executando modelo dbt: {model_name}")

    dbt = dbtRunner()
    cli_args = [
        "run",
        "--select", model_name,
        "--project-dir", DBT_PROJECT_DIR,
        "--profiles-dir", os.path.expanduser("~/.dbt")
    ]

    if full_refresh:
        cli_args.append("--full-refresh")

    result = dbt.invoke(cli_args)

    if not result.success:
        logger.error(f"Falha ao executar modelo {model_name}: {result.exception}")
        raise result.exception

    return result

@task(name="validate_bigquery_table")
def validate_bigquery_table(dataset_id: str, table_id: str):
    """Valida se a tabela existe e tem dados recentes"""
    logger = get_run_logger()
    client = bigquery.Client()

    try:
        table_ref = f"{client.project}.{dataset_id}.{table_id}"
        table = client.get_table(table_ref)

        # Verificar se a tabela tem dados recentes (últimos 5 minutos)
        query = f"""
            SELECT COUNT(*) as record_count
            FROM `{table_ref}`
            WHERE TIMESTAMP_DIFF(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(), updated_at, MINUTE) <= 5
        """
        result = client.query(query).result()
        record_count = next(result).record_count

        if record_count == 0:
            logger.warning(f"Tabela {table_ref} não tem dados recentes")
            return False

        logger.info(f"Tabela {table_ref} validada com {record_count} registros recentes")
        return True

    except NotFound:
        logger.error(f"Tabela {dataset_id}.{table_id} não encontrada")
        return False
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Erro ao validar tabela {dataset_id}.{table_id}: {str(e)}")
        raise

@task(name="send_slack_alert")
def send_slack_alert(message: str, is_error: bool = True):
    """Envia alerta para Slack"""
    logger = get_run_logger()
    try:
        slack_webhook = SlackWebhook.load(SLACK_WEBHOOK_BLOCK)
        status = "❌ ERRO" if is_error else "✅ SUCESSO"
        slack_webhook.notify(f"{status} - Pipeline de dados em tempo real\n{message}")
        logger.info(f"Alerta enviado para Slack: {message}")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Falha ao enviar alerta para Slack: {str(e)}")

@task(name="generate_run_report")
def generate_run_report(success: bool, details: dict):
    """Gera relatório markdown do run"""
    logger = get_run_logger()

    status = "✅ SUCESSO" if success else "❌ FALHA"
    report = f"""
# Relatório de Execução do Pipeline em Tempo Real

**Status**: {status}
**Timestamp**: {details.get('timestamp', 'N/A')}

## Detalhes da Execução

- **Modelos Executados**: {', '.join(details.get('models', []))}
- **Duração**: {details.get('duration', 'N/A')} segundos
- **Registros Processados**: {details.get('records_processed', 'N/A')}

## Validações

- **Tabelas Validadas**: {', '.join(details.get('validated_tables', []))}
- **Problemas Encontrados**: {details.get('issues', 'Nenhum')}

## Observações

{details.get('observations', 'Nenhuma observação')}
    """

    create_markdown_artifact(
        key="realtime-pipeline-report",
        markdown=report,
        description="Relatório de execução do pipeline em tempo real"
    )
    logger.info("Relatório gerado com sucesso")

@flow(
    name="realtime-data-pipeline",
    task_runner=ConcurrentTaskRunner(),
    retries=1,
    retry_delay_seconds=60,
    timeout_seconds=1800
)
def realtime_data_pipeline():
    """Pipeline principal de dados em tempo real com processamento paralelo"""
    logger = get_run_logger()
    run_details = {
        "timestamp": str(datetime.datetime.utcnow()),
        "models": [],
        "validated_tables": [],
        "issues": [],
        "observations": ""
    }

    try:
        logger.info("Iniciando pipeline de dados em tempo real")

        # 1. Executar modelos dbt em paralelo
        with ConcurrentTaskRunner():
            # Camada raw (processamento inicial)
            raw_future = run_dbt_model.submit("raw_events")

            # Camada staging (processamento paralelo)
            staging_futures = [
                run_dbt_model.submit("stg_events"),
                run_dbt_model.submit("stg_llm_calls")
            ]

            # Camada marts (processamento paralelo)
            marts_futures = [
                run_dbt_model.submit("mart_product.realtime_metrics"),
                run_dbt_model.submit("mart_ai.llm_cost_realtime")
            ]

            # Aguardar conclusão das tarefas
            raw_result = raw_future.result()
            staging_results = [f.result() for f in staging_futures]
            marts_results = [f.result() for f in marts_futures]

            run_details["models"] = [
                "raw_events",
                "stg_events", "stg_llm_calls",
                "mart_product.realtime_metrics", "mart_ai.llm_cost_realtime"
            ]

        # 2. Validar tabelas no BigQuery
        validation_results = [
            validate_bigquery_table("mart_product", "realtime_metrics"),
            validate_bigquery_table("mart_ai", "llm_cost_realtime")
        ]

        validated_tables = [
            "mart_product.realtime_metrics" if validation_results[0] else None,
            "mart_ai.llm_cost_realtime" if validation_results[1] else None
        ]
        run_details["validated_tables"] = [t for t in validated_tables if t]

        if not all(validation_results):
            issues = []
            if not validation_results[0]:
                issues.append("mart_product.realtime_metrics não validada")
            if not validation_results[1]:
                issues.append("mart_ai.llm_cost_realtime não validada")
            run_details["issues"] = issues
            raise ValueError("Falha na validação de tabelas")

        # 3. Gerar relatório de execução
        run_details["duration"] = (datetime.datetime.utcnow() -
                                 datetime.datetime.fromisoformat(run_details["timestamp"])).seconds
        run_details["records_processed"] = "Estimativa: ~1000 registros/minuto"
        run_details["observations"] = "Pipeline executado com sucesso em modo Hive para processamento paralelo"

        generate_run_report(success=True, details=run_details)
        send_slack_alert("Pipeline de dados em tempo real concluído com sucesso", is_error=False)

        logger.info("Pipeline concluído com sucesso")
        return True

    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Falha no pipeline: {str(e)}")
        run_details["issues"].append(str(e))
        run_details["observations"] = "Pipeline falhou durante a execução"

        generate_run_report(success=False, details=run_details)
        send_slack_alert(f"Falha no pipeline de dados em tempo real: {str(e)}")

        raise

if __name__ == "__main__":
    realtime_data_pipeline()
```

**/prefect/flows/monitoring.py**
```python
import time
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from prefect import flow, task, get_run_logger
from prefect.blocks.notifications import SlackWebhook
from google.cloud import bigquery
from google.api_core.exceptions import NotFound

# Configurações
SLACK_WEBHOOK_BLOCK = "slack-alerts"
MONITORING_INTERVAL_MINUTES = 5

@task(name="check_table_freshness")
def check_table_freshness(dataset_id: str, table_id: str, max_minutes_old: int = 10):
    """Verifica se a tabela tem dados recentes"""
    logger = get_run_logger()
    client = bigquery.Client()

    try:
        table_ref = f"{client.project}.{dataset_id}.{table_id}"
        query = f"""
            SELECT
                TIMESTAMP_DIFF(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(), MAX(updated_at), MINUTE) as minutes_old
            FROM `{table_ref}`
        """
        result = client.query(query).result()
        minutes_old = next(result).minutes_old

        if minutes_old > max_minutes_old:
            logger.warning(
                f"Tabela {dataset_id}.{table_id} não atualizada. "
                f"Última atualização: {minutes_old} minutos atrás"
            )
            return False

        logger.info(f"Tabela {dataset_id}.{table_id} atualizada ({minutes_old} minutos atrás)")
        return True

    except NotFound:
        logger.error(f"Tabela {dataset_id}.{table_id} não encontrada")
        return False
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Erro ao verificar frescor da tabela {dataset_id}.{table_id}: {str(e)}")
        raise

@task(name="check_pipeline_sla")
def check_pipeline_sla(expected_interval_minutes: int = 5):
    """Verifica se o pipeline está executando dentro do SLA"""
    logger = get_run_logger()
    client = bigquery.Client()

    try:
        # Verificar última execução do pipeline
        query = """
            SELECT
                TIMESTAMP_DIFF(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(), MAX(updated_at), MINUTE) as minutes_since_last_run
            FROM `mart_product.realtime_metrics`
        """
        result = client.query(query).result()
        minutes_since_last_run = next(result).minutes_since_last_run

        if minutes_since_last_run > expected_interval_minutes * 2:
            logger.warning(
                f"Pipeline fora do SLA. Última execução: {minutes_since_last_run} minutos atrás. "
                f"SLA esperado: {expected_interval_minutes} minutos"
            )
            return False

        logger.info(f"Pipeline dentro do SLA ({minutes_since_last_run} minutos desde última execução)")
        return True

    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Erro ao verificar SLA do pipeline: {str(e)}")
        raise

@task(name="send_monitoring_alert")
def send_monitoring_alert(message: str):
    """Envia alerta de monitoramento para Slack"""
    logger = get_run_logger()
    try:
        slack_webhook = SlackWebhook.load(SLACK_WEBHOOK_BLOCK)
        slack_webhook.notify(f"🚨 ALERTA DE MONITORAMENTO - Pipeline de Dados\n{message}")
        logger.info(f"Alerta de monitoramento enviado: {message}")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Falha ao enviar alerta de monitoramento: {str(e)}")

@flow(name="realtime-pipeline-monitoring")
def realtime_pipeline_monitoring():
    """Monitoramento contínuo do pipeline em tempo real"""
    logger = get_run_logger()

    while True:
        try:
            logger.info("Iniciando ciclo de monitoramento")

            # Verificar frescor das tabelas principais
            tables_to_check = [
                ("mart_product", "realtime_metrics", 10),
                ("mart_ai", "llm_cost_realtime", 10)
            ]

            all_tables_fresh = True
            for dataset_id, table_id, max_minutes in tables_to_check:
                if not check_table_freshness(dataset_id, table_id, max_minutes):
                    all_tables_fresh = False
                    send_monitoring_alert(
                        f"Tabela {dataset_id}.{table_id} não está sendo atualizada. "
                        f"Última atualização há mais de {max_minutes} minutos."
                    )

            # Verificar SLA do pipeline
            if not check_pipeline_sla():
                send_monitoring_alert(
                    "Pipeline de dados em tempo real fora do SLA. "
                    "Não está executando com a frequência esperada."
                )

            if all_tables_fresh:
                logger.info("Todas as verificações de monitoramento passaram")

            # Aguardar próximo ciclo
            time.sleep(MONITORING_INTERVAL_MINUTES * 60)

        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Erro no monitoramento: {str(e)}")
            send_monitoring_alert(f"Erro no monitoramento do pipeline: {str(e)}")
            time.sleep(60)  # Aguardar antes de tentar novamente

if __name__ == "__main__":
    realtime_pipeline_monitoring()
```

services:

      - prefect-server

volumes:

  prefect_data:

    driver: bridge

## 7. Configuração de Alertas

**/monitoring/alerts.py**
```python
from prefect.blocks.notifications import SlackWebhook
from google.cloud import bigquery
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

class DataPipelineAlerts:
    def __init__(self):
        self.slack_webhook = SlackWebhook.load("slack-alerts")
        self.bq_client = bigquery.Client()

    def check_data_quality(self):
        """Verificar qualidade dos dados nas tabelas principais"""
        issues = []

        # Verificar completude
        completeness_query = """
            SELECT
                COUNT(*) as null_count,
                COUNT(*) * 100.0 / (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM `{table}`) as null_percentage
            FROM `{table}`
            WHERE {field} IS NULL
        """

        tables_to_check = [
            {
                "table": "mart_product.realtime_metrics",
                "fields": ["metric_key", "metric_date", "unique_visitors"],
                "max_null_percentage": 1
            },
            {
                "table": "mart_ai.llm_cost_realtime",
                "fields": ["call_id", "timestamp", "model", "tokens_input"],
                "max_null_percentage": 1
            }
        ]

        for table_config in tables_to_check:
            for field in table_config["fields"]:
                query = completeness_query.format(
                    table=table_config["table"],
                    field=field
                )
                result = self.bq_client.query(query).result()
                row = next(result)

                if row.null_percentage > table_config["max_null_percentage"]:
                    issues.append(
                        f"Completude violada em {table_config['table']}.{field}: "
                        f"{row.null_percentage:.2f}% de valores nulos (limite: {table_config['max_null_percentage']}%)"
                    )

        # Verificar unicidade
        uniqueness_query = """
            SELECT
                {field} as duplicate_value,
                COUNT(*) as duplicate_count
            FROM `{table}`
            GROUP BY {field}
            HAVING COUNT(*) > 1
        """

        uniqueness_checks = [
            {"table": "mart_product.realtime_metrics", "field": "metric_key"},
            {"table": "mart_ai.llm_cost_realtime", "field": "call_id"}
        ]

        for check in uniqueness_checks:
            query = uniqueness_query.format(
                table=check["table"],
                field=check["field"]
            )
            results = self.bq_client.query(query).result()

            for row in results:
                issues.append(
                    f"Unicidade violada em {check['table']}.{check['field']}: "
                    f"Valor '{row.duplicate_value}' aparece {row.duplicate_count} vezes"
                )

        return issues

    def check_sla_compliance(self):
        """Verificar conformidade com SLAs"""
        issues = []

        # Verificar SLA de atualização para métricas de produto (diário até 08h)
        product_sla_query = """
            SELECT
                TIMESTAMP_DIFF(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(), MAX(updated_at), HOUR) as hours_since_update
            FROM `mart_product.realtime_metrics`
            WHERE metric_date = CURRENT_DATE()
        """
        result = self.bq_client.query(product_sla_query).result()
        hours_since_update = next(result).hours_since_update

        if hours_since_update > 24:
            issues.append(
                f"SLA violado: Métricas de produto não atualizadas há {hours_since_update} horas. "
                "Esperado: atualização diária até 08h"
            )

        # Verificar SLA de atualização para custo LLM (a cada 1h)
        llm_sla_query = """
            SELECT
                TIMESTAMP_DIFF(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(), MAX(updated_at), MINUTE) as minutes_since_update
            FROM `mart_ai.llm_cost_realtime`
        """
        result = self.bq_client.query(llm_sla_query).result()
        minutes_since_update = next(result).minutes_since_update

        if minutes_since_update > 60:
            issues.append(
                f"SLA violado: Custo LLM não atualizado há {minutes_since_update} minutos. "
                "Esperado: atualização a cada 60 minutos"
            )

        return issues

    def send_alert(self, message: str, is_error: bool = True):
        """Enviar alerta para Slack"""
        status = "❌ ERRO" if is_error else "⚠️ ALERTA"
        try:
            self.slack_webhook.notify(f"{status} - Pipeline de Dados\n{message}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Falha ao enviar alerta: {str(e)}")

    def run_checks(self):
        """Executar todas as verificações e enviar alertas"""
        issues = []

        # Verificar qualidade dos dados
        quality_issues = self.check_data_quality()
        if quality_issues:
            issues.extend(quality_issues)

        # Verificar conformidade com SLAs
        sla_issues = self.check_sla_compliance()
        if sla_issues:
            issues.extend(sla_issues)

        # Enviar alertas se houver problemas
        if issues:
            alert_message = "Problemas detectados no pipeline de dados:\n" + "\n".join(
                [f"• {issue}" for issue in issues]
            )
            self.send_alert(alert_message)
            return False

        # Se tudo estiver OK, enviar mensagem de sucesso
        self.send_alert(
            "✅ Todas as verificações de qualidade e SLA passaram com sucesso",
            is_error=False
        )
        return True
```

## 8. Sincronização com DataHub

**/monitoring/datahub_sync.py**
```python
from datahub.emitter.mce_builder import (
    make_dataset_urn,
    make_data_platform_urn,
    make_dataset_properties,
    make_dataset_usage_statistics
)
from datahub.emitter.rest_emitter import DatahubRestEmitter
from datahub.metadata.schema_classes import (
    DatasetSnapshotClass,
    MetadataChangeEventClass,
    DatasetPropertiesClass,
    DatasetUsageStatisticsClass
)
from google.cloud import bigquery
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import time

class DataHubSync:
    def __init__(self):
        # Configurar emissor para DataHub
        self.emitter = DatahubRestEmitter(
            gms_server="http://datahub-gms:8080"
        )
        self.bq_client = bigquery.Client()

    def get_table_metadata(self, dataset_id: str, table_id: str):
        """Obter metadados da tabela do BigQuery"""
        table_ref = f"{self.bq_client.project}.{dataset_id}.{table_id}"
        table = self.bq_client.get_table(table_ref)

        # Obter estatísticas de uso
        query = f"""
            SELECT
                COUNT(*) as record_count,
                TIMESTAMP_DIFF(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(), MAX(updated_at), HOUR) as hours_since_update
            FROM `{table_ref}`
        """
        result = self.bq_client.query(query).result()
        stats = next(result)

        return {
            "description": table.description or "",
            "columns": [col.name for col in table.schema],
            "record_count": stats.record_count,
            "last_updated": datetime.utcnow() - timedelta(hours=stats.hours_since_update),
            "schema": str(table.schema)
        }

    def emit_dataset_metadata(self, dataset_id: str, table_id: str):
        """Emitir metadados da tabela para DataHub"""
        metadata = self.get_table_metadata(dataset_id, table_id)

        # Criar URN do dataset
        dataset_urn = make_dataset_urn(
            platform="bigquery",
            name=f"{dataset_id}.{table_id}",
            env="PROD"
        )

        # Criar propriedades do dataset
        properties = DatasetPropertiesClass(
            description=metadata["description"],
            customProperties={
                "record_count": str(metadata["record_count"]),
                "last_updated": metadata["last_updated"].isoformat(),
                "schema": metadata["schema"]
            }
        )

        # Criar snapshot do dataset
        dataset_snapshot = DatasetSnapshotClass(
            urn=dataset_urn,
            aspects=[properties]
        )

        # Criar evento de mudança
        mce = MetadataChangeEventClass(
            proposedSnapshot=dataset_snapshot
        )

        # Emitir para DataHub
        self.emitter.emit(mce)
        print(f"Metadados emitidos para {dataset_id}.{table_id}")

    def emit_dataset_usage(self, dataset_id: str, table_id: str):
        """Emitir estatísticas de uso para DataHub"""
        table_ref = f"{self.bq_client.project}.{dataset_id}.{table_id}"

        # Obter estatísticas de uso (simplificado - em produção usar query history)
        query = f"""
            SELECT
                COUNT(*) as query_count,
                COUNT(DISTINCT user_email) as user_count
            FROM `region-us`.INFORMATION_SCHEMA.JOBS_BY_PROJECT
            WHERE
                query LIKE '%{table_ref}%'
                AND creation_time >= TIMESTAMP_SUB(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(), INTERVAL 24 HOUR)
        """
        result = self.bq_client.query(query).result()
        stats = next(result)

        # Criar URN do dataset
        dataset_urn = make_dataset_urn(
            platform="bigquery",
            name=f"{dataset_id}.{table_id}",
            env="PROD"
        )

        # Criar estatísticas de uso
        usage_stats = DatasetUsageStatisticsClass(
            timestampMillis=int(time.time() * 1000),
            uniqueUserCount=stats.user_count,
            totalSqlQueries=stats.query_count,
            topSqlQueries=[]
        )

        # Criar evento de mudança
        mce = MetadataChangeEventClass(
            proposedSnapshot=DatasetSnapshotClass(
                urn=dataset_urn,
                aspects=[usage_stats]
            )
        )

        # Emitir para DataHub
        self.emitter.emit(mce)
        print(f"Estatísticas de uso emitidas para {dataset_id}.{table_id}")

    def sync_all_datasets(self):
        """Sincronizar todos os datasets relevantes com DataHub"""
        datasets = [
            ("mart_product", "realtime_metrics"),
            ("mart_ai", "llm_cost_realtime"),
            ("staging", "stg_events"),
            ("staging", "stg_llm_calls")
        ]

        for dataset_id, table_id in datasets:
            try:
                self.emit_dataset_metadata(dataset_id, table_id)
                self.emit_dataset_usage(dataset_id, table_id)
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"Erro ao sincronizar {dataset_id}.{table_id}: {str(e)}")
```

## Implementação do Modo Hive para Processamento Paralelo

O Modo Hive no BigQuery permite otimizar consultas em tabelas particionadas, especialmente para processamento paralelo. As principais otimizações implementadas:

1. **Particionamento Otimizado**:
   - Todas as tabelas nas camadas staging e marts são particionadas por data
   - Uso de `partition_by` no dbt para definir o particionamento

2. **Processamento Incremental**:
   - Modelos dbt configurados com `incremental_strategy: merge`
   - Filtros de tempo nas consultas incrementais usando a macro `get_realtime_window()`

3. **Hive Partitioning**:
   - Ativado através da macro `enable_hive_mode()`
   - Permite que o BigQuery otimize automaticamente consultas em tabelas particionadas

4. **Orquestração Paralela**:
   - Uso do `ConcurrentTaskRunner` no Prefect para executar modelos dbt em paralelo
   - Dependências entre camadas gerenciadas automaticamente

5. **Consultas Otimizadas**:
   - Uso de CTEs (Common Table Expressions) para melhorar a legibilidade e performance
   - Filtros aplicados o mais cedo possível nas consultas

## Monitoramento e Alertas

O sistema inclui um monitoramento abrangente com:

1. **Verificação de Frescor**:
   - Tabelas verificadas a cada 5 minutos
   - Alertas quando dados não são atualizados dentro do SLA

2. **Verificação de Qualidade**:
   - Testes de completude (valores nulos)
   - Testes de unicidade (chaves duplicadas)
   - Alertas quando limites são violados

3. **Conformidade com SLAs**:
   - Verificação de atualização diária para métricas de produto
   - Verificação de atualização horária para custo LLM

4. **Notificações**:
   - Alertas via Slack para problemas
   - Relatórios de execução gerados automaticamente

## Como Executar

1. **Configurar credenciais**:
   - Criar arquivo `secrets/gcp-credentials.json` com as credenciais do BigQuery
   - Configurar webhook do Slack no Prefect

2. **Iniciar serviços**:
   ```bash
   docker-compose up -d
   ```

3. **Configurar Airbyte**:
   - Acessar http://localhost:8000
   - Criar conexão com o conector custom `streaming_source.py`
   - Configurar destino para BigQuery

4. **Executar pipeline**:
   ```bash
   docker-compose exec prefect-server prefect deployment build prefect/flows/realtime_pipeline.py:realtime_data_pipeline -n production -q default
   docker-compose exec prefect-server prefect deployment apply realtime_data_pipeline-deployment.yaml
   docker-compose exec prefect-server prefect deployment run "realtime-data-pipeline/production"
   ```

5. **Iniciar monitoramento**:
   ```bash
   docker-compose exec monitoring python flows/monitoring.py
   ```

Este pipeline implementa um sistema de processamento de dados em tempo real com alta eficiência, utilizando o Modo Hive para processamento paralelo e garantindo estabilidade autônoma através de monitoramento contínuo e alertas proativos.

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Lead]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core: Arquitetura Revisada para Escalabilidade e Segurança

Vou propor uma arquitetura revisada com foco em escalabilidade e segurança, mantendo a autonomia do sistema. A estrutura seguirá princípios de microsserviços leves, containers e práticas de segurança por design.

## Estrutura de Diretórios Revisada

```
/diyapp-v12-core
├── /src
│   ├── /core                  # Núcleo autônomo
│   │   ├── autonomousEngine.js
│   │   ├── decisionMatrix.js
│   │   └── selfHealing.js
│   ├── /services              # Serviços modulares
│   │   ├── /apiGateway
│   │   ├── /authService
│   │   ├── /dataService
│   │   ├── /notificationService
│   │   └── /monitoringService
│   ├── /controllers           # Controladores REST
│   ├── /models                # Modelos de dados
│   ├── /middlewares           # Middlewares de segurança
│   ├── /utils                 # Utilitários
│   └── /config                # Configurações centralizadas
├── /public                    # Frontend
│   ├── index.html             # Dashboard principal
│   ├── /assets
│   └── /js
├── /docker                    # Configurações de container
├── /scripts                   # Scripts de automação
├── /tests                     # Testes automatizados
├── .env.example               # Exemplo de variáveis de ambiente
├── docker-compose.yml         # Orquestração de containers
├── package.json
└── README.md
```

## 1. Core Autônomo Revisado (src/core)

### autonomousEngine.js (Núcleo de Decisão)

```javascript
const { DecisionMatrix } = require('./decisionMatrix');
const { SelfHealing } = require('./selfHealing');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');
const { performance } = require('perf_hooks');

class AutonomousEngine {
  constructor() {
    this.decisionMatrix = new DecisionMatrix();
    this.selfHealing = new SelfHealing();
    this.serviceRegistry = new Map();
    this.lastHealthCheck = performance.now();
    this.healthCheckInterval = 30000; // 30 segundos
  }

  async initialize() {
    try {
      await this.registerCoreServices();
      await this.startHealthMonitoring();
      logger.info('Autonomous Engine initialized successfully');
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Autonomous Engine initialization failed', error);
      await this.selfHealing.triggerRecovery('engine_init_failure', error);
    }
  }

  async registerCoreServices() {
    // Registrar serviços essenciais
    this.serviceRegistry.set('apiGateway', {
      status: 'initializing',
      lastPing: performance.now(),
      dependencies: []
    });

    // Outros serviços serão registrados dinamicamente
  }

  async startHealthMonitoring() {
    setInterval(async () => {
      try {
        const now = performance.now();
        if (now - this.lastHealthCheck > this.healthCheckInterval) {
          await this.performHealthCheck();
          this.lastHealthCheck = now;
        }
      } catch (error) {
        logger.error('Health monitoring error', error);
      }
    }, 5000);
  }

  async performHealthCheck() {
    const services = Array.from(this.serviceRegistry.entries());
    const unhealthyServices = [];

    for (const [serviceName, serviceInfo] of services) {
      try {
        const isHealthy = await this.checkServiceHealth(serviceName);
        if (!isHealthy) {
          unhealthyServices.push(serviceName);
          logger.warn(`Service ${serviceName} is unhealthy`);
        }
      } catch (error) {
        logger.error(`Health check failed for ${serviceName}`, error);
        unhealthyServices.push(serviceName);
      }
    }

    if (unhealthyServices.length > 0) {
      await this.handleUnhealthyServices(unhealthyServices);
    }
  }

  async checkServiceHealth(serviceName) {
    // Implementação específica para cada serviço
    switch (serviceName) {
      case 'apiGateway':
        return this.checkAPIGatewayHealth();
      case 'authService':
        return this.checkAuthServiceHealth();
      // Outros serviços...
      default:
        return false;
    }
  }

  async handleUnhealthyServices(serviceNames) {
    for (const serviceName of serviceNames) {
      try {
        const recoveryResult = await this.selfHealing.recoverService(serviceName);
        if (!recoveryResult) {
          logger.error(`Failed to recover service ${serviceName}`);
          // Escalar para intervenção humana se necessário
        }
      } catch (error) {
        logger.error(`Recovery failed for ${serviceName}`, error);
      }
    }
  }

  async makeDecision(context) {
    try {
      const decision = await this.decisionMatrix.evaluate(context);
      logger.info(`Decision made: ${decision.action}`, { context, decision });
      return decision;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Decision making failed', error);
      throw error;
    }
  }
}

module.exports = new AutonomousEngine();
```

### decisionMatrix.js (Matriz de Decisão)

```javascript
const { performance } = require('perf_hooks');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');
const { RuleEngine } = require('../utils/ruleEngine');

class DecisionMatrix {
  constructor() {
    this.ruleEngine = new RuleEngine();
    this.decisionCache = new Map();
    this.cacheTTL = 300000; // 5 minutos
    this.initializeRules();
  }

  initializeRules() {
    // Regras de escalabilidade
    this.ruleEngine.addRule({
      name: 'scale_up_api_gateway',
      condition: (context) => context.requestRate > 1000 && context.cpuUsage < 80,
      action: () => ({ action: 'scale_up', target: 'apiGateway', priority: 'high' })
    });

    this.ruleEngine.addRule({
      name: 'scale_down_api_gateway',
      condition: (context) => context.requestRate < 200 && context.cpuUsage < 30,
      action: () => ({ action: 'scale_down', target: 'apiGateway', priority: 'medium' })
    });

    // Regras de segurança
    this.ruleEngine.addRule({
      name: 'block_suspicious_ip',
      condition: (context) => context.failedAuthAttempts > 5,
      action: (context) => ({
        action: 'block_ip',
        target: context.ipAddress,
        duration: 3600000 // 1 hora
      })
    });

    // Regras de auto-cura
    this.ruleEngine.addRule({
      name: 'restart_failed_service',
      condition: (context) => context.serviceStatus === 'failed' && context.restartAttempts < 3,
      action: (context) => ({
        action: 'restart_service',
        target: context.serviceName,
        priority: 'critical'
      })
    });
  }

  async evaluate(context) {
    const cacheKey = this.generateCacheKey(context);
    const cachedDecision = this.decisionCache.get(cacheKey);

    if (cachedDecision && (performance.now() - cachedDecision.timestamp < this.cacheTTL)) {
      return cachedDecision.decision;
    }

    try {
      const decision = await this.ruleEngine.evaluate(context);
      this.decisionCache.set(cacheKey, {
        decision,
        timestamp: performance.now()
      });
      return decision;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Decision evaluation failed', error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  generateCacheKey(context) {
    // Gerar uma chave única baseada no contexto
    return JSON.stringify({
      ...context,
      timestamp: undefined // Ignorar timestamp para cache
    });
  }
}

module.exports = DecisionMatrix;
```

### selfHealing.js (Auto-Cura)

```javascript
const { exec } = require('child_process');
const { promisify } = require('util');
const execAsync = promisify(exec);
const logger = require('../utils/logger');
const autonomousEngine = require('./autonomousEngine');

class SelfHealing {
  constructor() {
    this.recoveryAttempts = new Map();
    this.maxAttempts = 3;
    this.cooldownPeriod = 300000; // 5 minutos
  }

  async triggerRecovery(issueType, context) {
    try {
      const recoveryAction = this.determineRecoveryAction(issueType, context);

      if (!recoveryAction) {
        logger.warn(`No recovery action defined for issue type: ${issueType}`);
        return false;
      }

      const attemptKey = `${issueType}:${context.serviceName || 'system'}`;
      const attempts = this.recoveryAttempts.get(attemptKey) || 0;

      if (attempts >= this.maxAttempts) {
        logger.error(`Max recovery attempts reached for ${attemptKey}`);
        return false;
      }

      this.recoveryAttempts.set(attemptKey, attempts + 1);

      logger.info(`Attempting recovery for ${issueType}`, {
        action: recoveryAction,
        attempt: attempts + 1
      });

      const result = await this.executeRecoveryAction(recoveryAction, context);

      if (result.success) {
        this.recoveryAttempts.delete(attemptKey);
        logger.info(`Recovery successful for ${issueType}`);
        return true;
      } else {
        logger.error(`Recovery failed for ${issueType}`, result.error);
        return false;
      }
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Recovery trigger failed', error);
      return false;
    }
  }

  determineRecoveryAction(issueType, context) {
    const actions = {
      'engine_init_failure': { action: 'restart_engine', priority: 'critical' },
      'service_failure': { action: 'restart_service', target: context.serviceName },
      'high_cpu_usage': { action: 'scale_up', target: context.serviceName },
      'auth_failure': { action: 'rotate_credentials', target: 'authService' },
      'db_connection_failure': { action: 'reconnect_db', target: 'dataService' }
    };

    return actions[issueType] || null;
  }

  async executeRecoveryAction(action, context) {
    try {
      switch (action.action) {
        case 'restart_engine':
          return await this.restartEngine();
        case 'restart_service':
          return await this.restartService(action.target);
        case 'scale_up':
          return await this.scaleService(action.target, 'up');
        case 'scale_down':
          return await this.scaleService(action.target, 'down');
        case 'rotate_credentials':
          return await this.rotateCredentials();
        case 'reconnect_db':
          return await this.reconnectDatabase();
        default:
          return { success: false, error: `Unknown action: ${action.action}` };
      }
    } catch (error) {
      return { success: false, error };
    }
  }

  async restartEngine() {
    try {
      // Implementação específica para reiniciar o engine
      // Em um ambiente containerizado, isso poderia ser um restart do container
      logger.info('Restarting autonomous engine...');
      await execAsync('pm2 restart diyapp-engine');
      return { success: true };
    } catch (error) {
      return { success: false, error };
    }
  }

  async restartService(serviceName) {
    try {
      logger.info(`Restarting service ${serviceName}...`);
      await execAsync(`pm2 restart ${serviceName}`);
      return { success: true };
    } catch (error) {
      return { success: false, error };
    }
  }

  async scaleService(serviceName, direction) {
    try {
      logger.info(`Scaling ${direction} service ${serviceName}...`);
      const scaleCommand = direction === 'up'
        ? `pm2 scale ${serviceName} +1`
        : `pm2 scale ${serviceName} -1`;

      await execAsync(scaleCommand);
      return { success: true };
    } catch (error) {
      return { success: false, error };
    }
  }

  async rotateCredentials() {
    try {
      logger.info('Rotating credentials...');
      // Implementação específica para rotação de credenciais
      // Poderia envolver chamadas para serviços de vault ou gerenciadores de segredos
      return { success: true };
    } catch (error) {
      return { success: false, error };
    }
  }

  async reconnectDatabase() {
    try {
      logger.info('Reconnecting to database...');
      // Implementação específica para reconexão com o banco de dados
      const db = require('../models');
      await db.sequelize.authenticate();
      return { success: true };
    } catch (error) {
      return { success: false, error };
    }
  }

  async recoverService(serviceName) {
    const context = { serviceName };
    return this.triggerRecovery('service_failure', context);
  }
}

module.exports = SelfHealing;
```

## 2. Serviços Modulares (src/services)

### apiGateway/index.js (API Gateway com Rate Limiting)

```javascript
const express = require('express');
const { createProxyMiddleware } = require('http-proxy-middleware');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const cors = require('cors');
const logger = require('../../utils/logger');
const { authenticate } = require('../../middlewares/auth');
const autonomousEngine = require('../../core/autonomousEngine');

class APIGateway {
  constructor() {
    this.app = express();
    this.port = process.env.API_GATEWAY_PORT || 3000;
    this.services = {
      auth: process.env.AUTH_SERVICE_URL || 'http://localhost:3001',
      data: process.env.DATA_SERVICE_URL || 'http://localhost:3002',
      notification: process.env.NOTIFICATION_SERVICE_URL || 'http://localhost:3003'
    };

    this.initializeMiddleware();
    this.initializeRoutes();
    this.initializeHealthCheck();
  }

  initializeMiddleware() {
    // Segurança básica
    this.app.use(helmet());
    this.app.use(cors({
      origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS.split(',') : '*',
      methods: ['GET', 'POST', 'PUT', 'DELETE', 'OPTIONS'],
      allowedHeaders: ['Content-Type', 'Authorization']
    }));

    // Rate limiting
    const limiter = rateLimit({
      windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
      max: 1000, // limite de requisições por IP
      message: 'Too many requests from this IP, please try again later',
      standardHeaders: true,
      legacyHeaders: false,
      keyGenerator: (req) => {
        return req.ip + (req.headers['x-api-key'] || '');
      },
      skip: (req) => {
        // Não aplicar rate limiting para health checks
        return req.path === '/health';
      }
    });

    this.app.use(limiter);

    // Logging
    this.app.use((req, res, next) => {
      logger.info(`${req.method} ${req.path}`, {
        ip: req.ip,
        userAgent: req.get('User-Agent'),
        query: req.query
      });
      next();
    });

    // Body parsing
    this.app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
    this.app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));
  }

  initializeRoutes() {
    // Health check
    this.app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
      res.status(200).json({ status: 'healthy' });
    });

    // Autenticação
    this.app.use('/auth', authenticate, createProxyMiddleware({
      target: this.services.auth,
      changeOrigin: true,
      pathRewrite: { '^/auth': '' },
      onProxyReq: (proxyReq, req) => {
        // Adicionar headers de autenticação
        if (req.user) {
          proxyReq.setHeader('x-user-id', req.user.id);
          proxyReq.setHeader('x-user-roles', req.user.roles.join(','));
        }
      }
    }));

    // Rotas protegidas
    this.app.use('/api', authenticate, (req, res, next) => {
      // Verificar permissões baseadas em roles
      if (!req.user.roles.includes('user')) {
        return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });
      }
      next();
    });

    // Data Service
    this.app.use('/api/data', createProxyMiddleware({
      target: this.services.data,
      changeOrigin: true,
      pathRewrite: { '^/api/data': '' },
      onProxyReq: (proxyReq, req) => {
        proxyReq.setHeader('x-request-id', req.id);
      }
    }));

    // Notification Service
    this.app.use('/api/notifications', createProxyMiddleware({
      target: this.services.notification,
      changeOrigin: true,
      pathRewrite: { '^/api/notifications': '' }
    }));

    // Rota para decisões autônomas
    this.app.post('/api/decide', authenticate, async (req, res) => {
      try {
        if (!req.user.roles.includes('admin')) {
          return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });
        }

        const decision = await autonomousEngine.makeDecision(req.body);
        res.json(decision);
      } catch (error) {
        logger.error('Decision endpoint error', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Decision making failed' });
      }
    });

    // Rota 404
    this.app.use('*', (req, res) => {
      res.status(404).json({ error: 'Not Found' });
    });
  }

  initializeHealthCheck() {
    setInterval(async () => {
      try {
        const isHealthy = await this.checkHealth();
        if (!isHealthy) {
          logger.error('API Gateway health check failed');
          // O autonomousEngine irá detectar e tentar recuperar
        }
      } catch (error) {
        logger.error('Health check error', error);
      }
    }, 30000);
  }

  async checkHealth() {
    try {
      // Verificar conexão com serviços downstream
      const checks = await Promise.all(
        Object.entries(this.services).map(async ([name, url]) => {
          try {
            const response = await fetch(`${url}/health`);
            return response.ok;
          } catch (error) {
            logger.error(`Health check failed for ${name} service`, error);
            return false;
          }
        })
      );

      return checks.every(check => check);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('API Gateway health check failed', error);
      return false;
    }
  }

  async start() {
    try {
      await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        this.server = this.app.listen(this.port, () => {
          logger.info(`API Gateway running on port ${this.port}`);
          resolve();
        });

        this.server.on('error', (error) => {
          logger.error('API Gateway failed to start', error);
          reject(error);
        });
      });

      // Registrar no autonomousEngine
      autonomousEngine.serviceRegistry.set('apiGateway', {
        status: 'running',
        lastPing: performance.now(),
        port: this.port
      });
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to start API Gateway', error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async stop() {
    try {
      if (this.server) {
        await new Promise((resolve) => {
          this.server.close(() => {
            logger.info('API Gateway stopped');
            resolve();
          });
        });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Error stopping API Gateway', error);
      throw error;
    }
  }
}

module.exports = new APIGateway();
```

### authService/index.js (Serviço de Autenticação com JWT)

```javascript
const express = require('express');
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const bcrypt = require('bcrypt');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const logger = require('../../utils/logger');
const { User } = require('../../models');
const autonomousEngine = require('../../core/autonomousEngine');

class AuthService {
  constructor() {
    this.app = express();
    this.port = process.env.AUTH_SERVICE_PORT || 3001;
    this.jwtSecret = process.env.JWT_SECRET || uuidv4();
    this.jwtExpiry = process.env.JWT_EXPIRY || '1h';
    this.refreshTokenExpiry = process.env.REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRY || '7d';

    this.initializeMiddleware();
    this.initializeRoutes();
    this.initializeHealthCheck();
  }

  initializeMiddleware() {
    this.app.use(helmet());
    this.app.use(express.json());

    // Rate limiting para endpoints de autenticação
    const authLimiter = rateLimit({
      windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
      max: 20, // limite de tentativas por IP
      message: 'Too many authentication attempts, please try again later',
      standardHeaders: true,
      legacyHeaders: false
    });

    this.app.use('/auth/login', authLimiter);
    this.app.use('/auth/refresh', authLimiter);
  }

  initializeRoutes() {
    // Health check
    this.app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
      res.status(200).json({ status: 'healthy' });
    });

    // Login
    this.app.post('/auth/login', async (req, res) => {
      try {
        const { email, password } = req.body;

        if (!email || !password) {
          return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Email and password are required' });
        }

        const user = await User.findOne({ where: { email } });
        if (!user) {
          // Simular tempo de resposta para evitar enumeração de usuários
          await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500));
          return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid credentials' });
        }

        const isPasswordValid = await bcrypt.compare(password, user.password);
        if (!isPasswordValid) {
          // Registrar tentativa falha para possível bloqueio
          await this.recordFailedAttempt(req.ip, email);

          return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid credentials' });
        }

        // Gerar tokens
        const accessToken = this.generateAccessToken(user);
        const refreshToken = this.generateRefreshToken(user);

        // Atualizar último login
        await user.update({ lastLogin: new Date() });

        res.json({
          accessToken,
          refreshToken,
          user: {
            id: user.id,
            email: user.email,
            roles: user.roles
          }
        });
      } catch (error) {
        logger.error('Login error', error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Authentication failed' });
      }
    });

    // Refresh token
    this.app.post('/auth/refresh', async (req, res) => {
      try {
        const { refreshToken } = req.body;

        if (!refreshToken) {
          return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Refresh token is required' });
        }

        const decoded = jwt.verify(refreshToken, this.jwtSecret);
        const user = await User.findByPk(decoded.id);

        if (!user) {
          return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid refresh token' });
        }

        // Gerar novo access token
        const accessToken = this.generateAccessToken(user);

        res.json({ accessToken });
      } catch (error) {
        logger.error('Refresh token error', error);
        res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid refresh token' });
      }
    });

    // Rota 404
    this.app.use('*', (req, res) => {
      res.status(404).json({ error: 'Not Found' });
    });
  }

  generateAccessToken(user) {
    return jwt.sign(
      {
        id: user.id,
        email: user.email,
        roles: user.roles
      },
      this.jwtSecret,
      { expiresIn: this.jwtExpiry }
    );
  }

  generateRefreshToken(user) {
    return jwt.sign(
      { id: user.id },
      this.jwtSecret,
      { expiresIn: this.refreshTokenExpiry }
    );
  }

  async recordFailedAttempt(ip, email) {
    try {
      // Implementação para registrar tentativas falhas
      // Poderia ser em um banco de dados ou cache
      const context = {
        ipAddress: ip,
        email,
        failedAuthAttempts: 1,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      };

      // Notificar o autonomousEngine para possível bloqueio
      await autonomousEngine.makeDecision({
        type: 'security_event',
        event: 'failed_auth_attempt',
        ...context
      });
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to record failed attempt', error);
    }
  }

  initializeHealthCheck() {
    setInterval(async () => {
      try {
        const isHealthy = await this.checkHealth();
        if (!isHealthy) {
          logger.error('Auth Service health check failed');
        }
      } catch (error) {
        logger.error('Auth Service health check error', error);
      }
    }, 30000);
  }

  async checkHealth() {
    try {
      // Verificar conexão com o banco de dados
      await User.findOne({ where: { id: 1 } });
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Auth Service health check failed', error);
      return false;
    }
  }

  async start() {
    try {
      await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        this.server = this.app.listen(this.port, () => {
          logger.info(`Auth Service running on port ${this.port}`);
          resolve();
        });

        this.server.on('error', (error) => {
          logger.error('Auth Service failed to start', error);
          reject(error);
        });
      });

      // Registrar no autonomousEngine
      autonomousEngine.serviceRegistry.set('authService', {
        status: 'running',
        lastPing: performance.now(),
        port: this.port
      });
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to start Auth Service', error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async stop() {
    try {
      if (this.server) {
        await new Promise((resolve) => {
          this.server.close(() => {
            logger.info('Auth Service stopped');
            resolve();
          });
        });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Error stopping Auth Service', error);
      throw error;
    }
  }
}

module.exports = new AuthService();
```

## 3. Middlewares de Segurança (src/middlewares)

### auth.js (Autenticação e Autorização)

```javascript
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');
const { User } = require('../models');
const autonomousEngine = require('../core/autonomousEngine');

const jwtSecret = process.env.JWT_SECRET;

const authenticate = async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    // Extrair token do header Authorization
    const authHeader = req.headers['authorization'];
    const token = authHeader && authHeader.split(' ')[1];

    if (!token) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Access token required' });
    }

    // Verificar token
    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, jwtSecret);

    // Buscar usuário no banco de dados
    const user = await User.findByPk(decoded.id);

    if (!user) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'User not found' });
    }

    // Verificar se o token foi revogado (implementação opcional)
    if (user.tokenRevoked) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Token revoked' });
    }

    // Adicionar usuário ao request
    req.user = {
      id: user.id,
      email: user.email,
      roles: user.roles
    };

    // Registrar atividade do usuário
    await this.logUserActivity(req);

    next();
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Authentication error', error);

    // Notificar o autonomousEngine sobre falha de autenticação
    await autonomousEngine.makeDecision({
      type: 'security_event',
      event: 'authentication_failure',
      ip: req.ip,
      userAgent: req.get('User-Agent'),
      error: error.message
    });

    if (error.name === 'JsonWebTokenError') {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid token' });
    }

    if (error.name === 'TokenExpiredError') {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Token expired' });
    }

    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Authentication failed' });
  }
};

const authorize = (roles = []) => {
  return (req, res, next) => {
    if (!req.user) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
    }

    // Verificar se o usuário tem pelo menos uma das roles requeridas
    const hasRole = roles.some(role => req.user.roles.includes(role));

    if (!hasRole) {
      logger.warn(`Unauthorized access attempt by ${req.user.email}`, {
        requiredRoles: roles,
        userRoles: req.user.roles
      });

      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });
    }

    next();
  };
};

const logUserActivity = async (req) => {
  try {
    // Implementação para registrar atividade do usuário
    // Poderia ser em um banco de dados ou serviço de logging
    const activity = {
      userId: req.user.id,
      ipAddress: req.ip,
      userAgent: req.get('User-Agent'),
      path: req.path,
      method: req.method,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    };

    // Notificar o autonomousEngine sobre a atividade
    await autonomousEngine.makeDecision({
      type: 'user_activity',
      ...activity
    });

    logger.info('User activity logged', activity);
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Failed to log user activity', error);
  }
};

module.exports = {
  authenticate,
  authorize
};
```

### security.js (Middlewares de Segurança Adicionais)

```javascript
const helmet = require('helmet');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const { body, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');
const autonomousEngine = require('../core/autonomousEngine');

// Configuração do Helmet para segurança de headers
const helmetConfig = helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'", "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'", "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:", "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net"],
      fontSrc: ["'self'", "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'", "https://*.diyapp.com"],
      frameAncestors: ["'none'"],
      formAction: ["'self'"],
      upgradeInsecureRequests: []
    }
  },
  hsts: {
    maxAge: 31536000, // 1 ano
    includeSubDomains: true,
    preload: true
  },
  referrerPolicy: { policy: 'same-origin' },
  frameguard: { action: 'deny' }
});

// Rate limiting para endpoints sensíveis
const apiLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
  max: 100, // limite de requisições por IP
  message: 'Too many requests from this IP, please try again later',
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
  keyGenerator: (req) => {
    return req.ip + (req.user ? req.user.id : '');
  },
  skip: (req) => {
    // Não aplicar rate limiting para health checks
    return req.path === '/health';
  }
});

// Validação de entrada para prevenir injeção
const validateInput = (validations) => {
  return async (req, res, next) => {
    await Promise.all(validations.map(validation => validation.run(req)));

    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (!errors.isEmpty()) {
      logger.warn('Input validation failed', {
        errors: errors.array(),
        path: req.path,
        method: req.method
      });

      // Notificar o autonomousEngine sobre validação falha
      await autonomousEngine.makeDecision({
        type: 'security_event',
        event: 'input_validation_failure',
        path: req.path,
        errors: errors.array()
      });

      return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
    }

    next();
  };
};

// Proteção contra CSRF (Cross-Site Request Forgery)
const csrfProtection = (req, res, next) => {
  // Em uma implementação real, usaríamos um token CSRF
  // Esta é uma implementação simplificada
  if (req.method === 'GET') {
    return next();
  }

  const csrfToken = req.headers['x-csrf-token'];
  const sessionToken = req.session?.csrfToken;

  if (!csrfToken || csrfToken !== sessionToken) {
    logger.warn('CSRF token validation failed', {
      path: req.path,
      method: req.method
    });

    // Notificar o autonomousEngine sobre falha de CSRF
    await autonomousEngine.makeDecision({
      type: 'security_event',
      event: 'csrf_validation_failure',
      path: req.path,
      ip: req.ip
    });

    return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Invalid CSRF token' });
  }

  next();
};

// Proteção contra ataques de força bruta
const bruteForceProtection = async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const ip = req.ip;
    const path = req.path;

    // Verificar se o IP está bloqueado
    const isBlocked = await checkIfIpBlocked(ip);

    if (isBlocked) {
      logger.warn(`Blocked request from IP ${ip} due to brute force protection`);
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Too many requests, please try again later' });
    }

    // Verificar tentativas recentes
    const recentAttempts = await getRecentAttempts(ip, path);

    if (recentAttempts >= 10) {
      // Bloquear IP
      await blockIp(ip);

      // Notificar o autonomousEngine
      await autonomousEngine.makeDecision({
        type: 'security_event',
        event: 'brute_force_detected',
        ip,
        path,
        attempts: recentAttempts
      });

      logger.warn(`IP ${ip} blocked due to brute force attempts on ${path}`);
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Too many requests, please try again later' });
    }

    // Registrar tentativa
    await recordAttempt(ip, path);

    next();
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Brute force protection error', error);
    next();
  }
};

// Funções auxiliares para proteção contra força bruta
const checkIfIpBlocked = async (ip) => {
  // Implementação real usaria Redis ou banco de dados
  return false;
};

const getRecentAttempts = async (ip, path) => {
  // Implementação real contaria tentativas recentes
  return 0;
};

const blockIp = async (ip) => {
  // Implementação real bloquearia o IP
  logger.info(`Blocking IP ${ip}`);
};

const recordAttempt = async (ip, path) => {
  // Implementação real registraria a tentativa
  logger.info(`Recording attempt from IP ${ip} on ${path}`);
};

module.exports = {
  helmetConfig,
  apiLimiter,
  validateInput,
  csrfProtection,
  bruteForceProtection
};
```

## 4. Configuração de Banco de Dados (src/models)

### index.js (Configuração do Sequelize)

```javascript
const { Sequelize } = require('sequelize');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');
const autonomousEngine = require('../core/autonomousEngine');

const env = process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development';
const config = require('../config/database')[env];

const sequelize = new Sequelize(config.database, config.username, config.password, {
  host: config.host,
  dialect: config.dialect,
  logging: env === 'development' ? logger.debug.bind(logger) : false,
  pool: {
    max: 20,
    min: 0,
    acquire: 30000,
    idle: 10000
  },
  retry: {
    match: [
      /ETIMEDOUT/,
      /EHOSTUNREACH/,
      /ECONNRESET/,
      /ECONNREFUSED/,
      /ETIMEDOUT/,
      /ESOCKETTIMEDOUT/,
      /EHOSTUNREACH/,
      /EPIPE/,
      /EAI_AGAIN/,
      /SequelizeConnectionError/,
      /SequelizeConnectionRefusedError/,
      /SequelizeHostNotFoundError/,
      /SequelizeHostNotReachableError/,
      /SequelizeInvalidConnectionError/,
      /SequelizeConnectionTimedOutError/
    ],
    max: 5
  },
  dialectOptions: {
    ssl: config.dialectOptions?.ssl ? {
      require: true,
      rejectUnauthorized: false
    } : false
  }
});

// Testar conexão e registrar no autonomousEngine
sequelize.authenticate()
  .then(() => {
    logger.info('Database connection has been established successfully.');

    // Registrar no autonomousEngine
    autonomousEngine.serviceRegistry.set('database', {
      status: 'connected',
      lastPing: performance.now(),
      host: config.host
    });
  })
  .catch(err => {
    logger.error('Unable to connect to the database:', err);

    // Notificar o autonomousEngine sobre falha de conexão
    autonomousEngine.makeDecision({
      type: 'system_event',
      event: 'database_connection_failure',
      error: err.message,
      host: config.host
    });
  });

// Modelos
const User = require('./user')(sequelize);
const AuditLog = require('./auditLog')(sequelize);
const ServiceStatus = require('./serviceStatus')(sequelize);

// Relacionamentos
User.hasMany(AuditLog, { foreignKey: 'userId' });
AuditLog.belongsTo(User, { foreignKey: 'userId' });

// Sincronizar modelos com o banco de dados
if (env === 'development') {
  sequelize.sync({ alter: true })
    .then(() => {
      logger.info('Database synchronized');
    })
    .catch(err => {
      logger.error('Database synchronization failed:', err);
    });
}

module.exports = {
  sequelize,
  User,
  AuditLog,
  ServiceStatus
};
```

### user.js (Modelo de Usuário)

```javascript
const { DataTypes } = require('sequelize');
const bcrypt = require('bcrypt');

module.exports = (sequelize) => {
  const User = sequelize.define('User', {
    id: {
      type: DataTypes.UUID,
      defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
      primaryKey: true
    },
    email: {
      type: DataTypes.STRING,
      allowNull: false,
      unique: true,
      validate: {
        isEmail: true
      }
    },
    password: {
      type: DataTypes.STRING,
      allowNull: false
    },
    roles: {
      type: DataTypes.ARRAY(DataTypes.STRING),
      defaultValue: ['user']
    },
    lastLogin: {
      type: DataTypes.DATE,
      allowNull: true
    },
    tokenRevoked: {
      type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
      defaultValue: false
    },
    failedLoginAttempts: {
      type: DataTypes.INTEGER,
      defaultValue: 0
    },
    accountLocked: {
      type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
      defaultValue: false
    },
    lockUntil: {
      type: DataTypes.DATE,
      allowNull: true
    }
  }, {
    hooks: {
      beforeCreate: async (user) => {
        user.password = await bcrypt.hash(user.password, 10);
      },
      beforeUpdate: async (user) => {
        if (user.changed('password')) {
          user.password = await bcrypt.hash(user.password, 10);
        }
      }
    },
    paranoid: true, // Habilitar soft delete
    indexes: [
      {
        unique: true,
        fields: ['email']
      },
      {
        fields: ['roles']
      }
    ]
  });

  // Método para comparar senhas
  User.prototype.comparePassword = async function(candidatePassword) {
    return await bcrypt.compare(candidatePassword, this.password);
  };

  // Método para incrementar tentativas de login falhas
  User.prototype.incrementFailedAttempts = async function() {
    this.failedLoginAttempts += 1;

    if (this.failedLoginAttempts >= 5) {
      this.accountLocked = true;
      this.lockUntil = new Date(Date.now() + 3600000); // Bloquear por 1 hora
    }

    await this.save();
  };

  // Método para desbloquear conta
  User.prototype.unlockAccount = async function() {
    this.accountLocked = false;
    this.lockUntil = null;
    this.failedLoginAttempts = 0;
    await this.save();
  };

  return User;
};
```
