### 2. Simulador de Ingestão (Airbyte)

```python
# src/ingestion/airbyte_simulator.py
import json
import time
import random
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Generator, Dict, Any
from pydantic import BaseModel

class AirbyteMessage(BaseModel):
    type: str
    record: Dict[str, Any] = None
    state: Dict[str, Any] = None
    log: Dict[str, Any] = None

class AirbyteSimulator:
    def __init__(self, source_name: str, config: Dict[str, Any]):
        self.source_name = source_name
        self.config = config
        self.stream_names = config.get("streams", [])
        self.cursor_field = config.get("cursor_field", "timestamp")
        self.last_cursor = None

    def generate_record(self, stream_name: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Gera um registro simulado para o stream especificado"""
        base_data = {
            "id": random.randint(1, 1000000),
            "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
            "source": self.source_name,
            "stream": stream_name
        }

        if stream_name == "user_events":
            return {
                **base_data,
                "user_id": random.randint(1, 10000),
                "event_type": random.choice(["login", "logout", "purchase", "view"]),
                "metadata": {
                    "device": random.choice(["mobile", "desktop", "tablet"]),
                    "os": random.choice(["iOS", "Android", "Windows", "MacOS"])
                }
            }
        elif stream_name == "llm_calls":
            return {
                **base_data,
                "call_id": f"call_{random.randint(1, 100000)}",
                "model": random.choice(["gpt-4", "gpt-3.5", "claude-2"]),
                "tokens_input": random.randint(10, 1000),
                "tokens_output": random.randint(10, 1000),
                "latency_ms": random.randint(50, 2000),
                "status": random.choice(["success", "error", "timeout"])
            }
        elif stream_name == "api_logs":
            return {
                **base_data,
                "endpoint": random.choice(["/api/v1/users", "/api/v1/products", "/api/v1/orders"]),
                "method": random.choice(["GET", "POST", "PUT", "DELETE"]),
                "status_code": random.choice([200, 201, 400, 401, 404, 500]),
                "response_time_ms": random.randint(10, 5000)
            }

        return base_data

    def read_stream(self, stream_name: str) -> Generator[AirbyteMessage, None, None]:
        """Simula a leitura de um stream do Airbyte"""
        while True:
            record = self.generate_record(stream_name)
            self.last_cursor = record[self.cursor_field]

            yield AirbyteMessage(
                type="RECORD",
                record={
                    "stream": stream_name,
                    "data": record,
                    "emitted_at": int(time.time() * 1000)
                }
            )

            # Simula delay entre registros
            time.sleep(random.uniform(0.1, 1.0))

    def get_streams(self) -> Generator[AirbyteMessage, None, None]:
        """Simula a descoberta de streams"""
        for stream in self.stream_names:
            yield AirbyteMessage(
                type="CATALOG",
                record={
                    "streams": [
                        {
                            "name": stream,
                            "json_schema": {
                                "type": "object",
                                "properties": {
                                    "id": {"type": "integer"},
                                    "timestamp": {"type": "string", "format": "date-time"}
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    ]
                }
            )

    def sync(self) -> Generator[AirbyteMessage, None, None]:
        """Simula o processo de sincronização do Airbyte"""
        # Envia mensagem de início
        yield AirbyteMessage(
            type="LOG",
            log={"level": "INFO", "message": f"Starting sync for source {self.source_name}"}
        )

        # Envia mensagens de estado
        yield AirbyteMessage(
            type="STATE",
            state={"cursor": self.last_cursor} if self.last_cursor else {}
        )

        # Lê todos os streams
        for stream in self.stream_names:
            for message in self.read_stream(stream):
                yield message

        # Envia mensagem de conclusão
        yield AirbyteMessage(
            type="LOG",
            log={"level": "INFO", "message": f"Completed sync for source {self.source_name}"}
        )
```

### 3. Conector em Tempo Real

```python
# src/ingestion/realtime_connector.py
import json
import time
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional
from pydantic import BaseModel
from datetime import datetime
import threading
import queue
from src.ingestion.airbyte_simulator import AirbyteSimulator

class RealtimeConnector:
    def __init__(self, config: Dict[str, Any]):
        self.config = config
        self.simulator = AirbyteSimulator(
            source_name=config["source_name"],
            config=config
        )
        self.message_queue = queue.Queue(maxsize=1000)
        self.running = False
        self.worker_thread = None

    def start(self):
        """Inicia o conector em uma thread separada"""
        if not self.running:
            self.running = True
            self.worker_thread = threading.Thread(target=self._run, daemon=True)
            self.worker_thread.start()

    def stop(self):
        """Para o conector"""
        self.running = False
        if self.worker_thread:
            self.worker_thread.join()

    def _run(self):
        """Executa o processo de sincronização em tempo real"""
        for message in self.simulator.sync():
            if not self.running:
                break

            if message.type == "RECORD":
                # Adiciona metadados de processamento
                message.record["data"]["processing_timestamp"] = datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
                self.message_queue.put(message)

                # Simula processamento em lote
                if self.message_queue.qsize() >= self.config.get("batch_size", 100):
                    self._process_batch()

    def _process_batch(self):
        """Processa um lote de mensagens"""
        batch = []
        while not self.message_queue.empty() and len(batch) < self.config.get("batch_size", 100):
            batch.append(self.message_queue.get())

        if batch:
            # Aqui normalmente enviaríamos para um sistema de mensageria (Kafka, Pub/Sub)
            # ou diretamente para o warehouse
            print(f"Processed batch of {len(batch)} records")

    def get_message(self) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Obtém uma mensagem da fila (para processamento individual)"""
        try:
            message = self.message_queue.get_nowait()
            return message.dict()
        except queue.Empty:
            return None
```

### 4. Processador Paralelo (Modo Hive)

```python
# src/transformation/hive_mode_processor.py
import duckdb
import pandas as pd
from typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed
from datetime import datetime
import logging
from src.storage.duckdb_client import DuckDBClient

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class HiveModeProcessor:
    def __init__(self, config: Dict[str, Any]):
        self.config = config
        self.db_client = DuckDBClient(config["warehouse_path"])
        self.executor = ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=config.get("max_workers", 4))
        self.batch_size = config.get("batch_size", 1000)

    def process_in_parallel(self, records: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> bool:
        """
        Processa registros em paralelo usando o Modo Hive
        Divide os registros em batches e processa cada batch em uma thread separada
        """
        if not records:
            return True

        # Divide os registros em batches
        batches = [
            records[i:i + self.batch_size]
            for i in range(0, len(records), self.batch_size)
        ]

        futures = []
        for batch in batches:
            future = self.executor.submit(self._process_batch, batch)
            futures.append(future)

        # Aguarda a conclusão de todos os batches
        success = True
        for future in as_completed(futures):
            try:
                result = future.result()
                if not result:
                    success = False
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Error processing batch: {str(e)}")
                success = False

        return success

    def _process_batch(self, batch: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> bool:
        """Processa um batch de registros na camada raw"""
        try:
            # Determina o stream para saber qual tabela usar
            stream_name = batch[0]["record"]["stream"]
            table_name = f"raw_{stream_name}"

            # Converte para DataFrame
            df = pd.DataFrame([record["record"]["data"] for record in batch])

            # Adiciona metadados de ingestão
            df["_ingested_at"] = datetime.utcnow()
            df["_source"] = self.config["source_name"]

            # Insere no DuckDB (simulando BigQuery)
            self.db_client.insert_dataframe(table_name, df)

            logger.info(f"Processed batch of {len(batch)} records for {stream_name}")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error processing batch: {str(e)}")
            return False

    def transform_to_staging(self, stream_name: str) -> bool:
        """Transforma dados da camada raw para staging"""
        try:
            raw_table = f"raw_{stream_name}"
            staging_table = f"stg_{stream_name}"

            # Verifica se a tabela raw existe
            if not self.db_client.table_exists(raw_table):
                logger.warning(f"Raw table {raw_table} does not exist")
                return False

            # Cria a query de transformação baseada no stream
            transform_query = self._get_transform_query(stream_name)

            # Executa a transformação
            self.db_client.execute_query(f"""
                CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE {staging_table} AS
                {transform_query}
            """)

            logger.info(f"Transformed {raw_table} to {staging_table}")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error transforming {stream_name} to staging: {str(e)}")
            return False

    def _get_transform_query(self, stream_name: str) -> str:
        """Retorna a query de transformação específica para cada stream"""
        if stream_name == "user_events":
            return f"""
                SELECT
                    id,
                    user_id,
                    event_type,
                    CAST(metadata AS JSON) as metadata,
                    timestamp,
                    processing_timestamp,
                    _ingested_at,
                    _source
                FROM {f"raw_{stream_name}"}
                WHERE timestamp IS NOT NULL
            """
        elif stream_name == "llm_calls":
            return f"""
                SELECT
                    id,
                    call_id,
                    model,
                    tokens_input,
                    tokens_output,
                    latency_ms,
                    status,
                    timestamp,
                    processing_timestamp,
                    _ingested_at,
                    _source
                FROM {f"raw_{stream_name}"}
                WHERE call_id IS NOT NULL
            """
        elif stream_name == "api_logs":
            return f"""
                SELECT
                    id,
                    endpoint,
                    method,
                    status_code,
                    response_time_ms,
                    timestamp,
                    processing_timestamp,
                    _ingested_at,
                    _source
                FROM {f"raw_{stream_name}"}
                WHERE endpoint IS NOT NULL
            """
        else:
            return f"SELECT * FROM {f'raw_{stream_name}'}"

    def create_marts(self) -> bool:
        """Cria as tabelas marts a partir dos dados staging"""
        try:
            # Mart de métricas de produto
            self.db_client.execute_query("""
                CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE mart_product_daily_metrics AS
                WITH daily_events AS (
                    SELECT
                        DATE(timestamp) as event_date,
                        user_id,
                        event_type,
                        COUNT(*) as event_count
                    FROM stg_user_events
                    GROUP BY 1, 2, 3
                ),
                daily_users AS (
                    SELECT
                        event_date,
                        COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) as active_users,
                        COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN event_type = 'login' THEN user_id END) as logins,
                        COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN event_type = 'purchase' THEN user_id END) as purchasers
                    FROM daily_events
                    GROUP BY 1
                )
                SELECT
                    event_date,
                    active_users,
                    logins,
                    purchasers,
                    logins::FLOAT / NULLIF(active_users, 0) as login_rate,
                    purchasers::FLOAT / NULLIF(active_users, 0) as conversion_rate
                FROM daily_users
                ORDER BY event_date
            """)

            # Mart de custos de LLM
            self.db_client.execute_query("""
                CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE mart_ai_llm_costs AS
                WITH cost_rates AS (
                    SELECT
                        model,
                        CASE
                            WHEN model = 'gpt-4' THEN 0.03
                            WHEN model = 'gpt-3.5' THEN 0.002
                            WHEN model = 'claude-2' THEN 0.01102
                            ELSE 0.01
                        END as input_cost_per_1k,
                        CASE
                            WHEN model = 'gpt-4' THEN 0.06
                            WHEN model = 'gpt-3.5' THEN 0.002
                            WHEN model = 'claude-2' THEN 0.03268
                            ELSE 0.02
                        END as output_cost_per_1k
                )
                SELECT
                    DATE(timestamp) as call_date,
                    model,
                    COUNT(*) as total_calls,
                    SUM(tokens_input) as total_input_tokens,
                    SUM(tokens_output) as total_output_tokens,
                    SUM(tokens_input) * (input_cost_per_1k / 1000) as input_cost,
                    SUM(tokens_output) * (output_cost_per_1k / 1000) as output_cost,
                    SUM(tokens_input) * (input_cost_per_1k / 1000) +
                    SUM(tokens_output) * (output_cost_per_1k / 1000) as total_cost,
                    AVG(latency_ms) as avg_latency_ms,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'success' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as success_count,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'error' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as error_count
                FROM stg_llm_calls
                JOIN cost_rates USING(model)
                GROUP BY 1, 2
                ORDER BY 1, 2
            """)

            # Mart de performance de API
            self.db_client.execute_query("""
                CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE mart_ops_api_performance AS
                SELECT
                    DATE(timestamp) as log_date,
                    endpoint,
                    method,
                    COUNT(*) as total_requests,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN status_code >= 200 AND status_code < 300 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as success_requests,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN status_code >= 400 AND status_code < 500 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as client_errors,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN status_code >= 500 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as server_errors,
                    AVG(response_time_ms) as avg_response_time,
                    PERCENTILE_CONT(0.95) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY response_time_ms) as p95_response_time
                FROM stg_api_logs
                GROUP BY 1, 2, 3
                ORDER BY 1, 2, 3
            """)

            logger.info("Created all mart tables")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error creating marts: {str(e)}")
            return False

    def shutdown(self):
        """Encerra o processador"""
        self.executor.shutdown(wait=True)
```

### 5. Cliente DuckDB (Simulando BigQuery)

```python
# src/storage/duckdb_client.py
import duckdb
import pandas as pd
from typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional
import logging

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class DuckDBClient:
    def __init__(self, db_path: str = ":memory:"):
        self.db_path = db_path
        self.conn = duckdb.connect(db_path)
        self._initialize_database()

    def _initialize_database(self):
        """Inicializa o banco de dados com as tabelas necessárias"""
        # Cria schemas para as camadas
        self.conn.execute("CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS raw")
        self.conn.execute("CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS staging")
        self.conn.execute("CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS marts")

        # Configura o DuckDB para melhor performance
        self.conn.execute("SET memory_limit='4GB'")
        self.conn.execute("SET threads TO 4")

    def table_exists(self, table_name: str) -> bool:
        """Verifica se uma tabela existe"""
        try:
            result = self.conn.execute(f"""
                SELECT COUNT(*) > 0 as exists
                FROM information_schema.tables
                WHERE table_schema || '.' || table_name = '{table_name}'
                OR table_name = '{table_name.split('.')[-1]}'
                AND table_schema = 'raw'
            """).fetchone()
            return result[0] if result else False
        except:
            return False

    def execute_query(self, query: str) -> Optional[pd.DataFrame]:
        """Executa uma query e retorna um DataFrame"""
        try:
            return self.conn.execute(query).df()
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error executing query: {str(e)}")
            return None

    def insert_dataframe(self, table_name: str, df: pd.DataFrame) -> bool:
        """Insere um DataFrame em uma tabela"""
        try:
            # Cria a tabela se não existir
            if not self.table_exists(table_name):
                self.conn.execute(f"CREATE TABLE {table_name} AS SELECT * FROM df LIMIT 0")
                logger.info(f"Created table {table_name}")

            # Insere os dados
            self.conn.register('temp_df', df)
            self.conn.execute(f"INSERT INTO {table_name} SELECT * FROM temp_df")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error inserting dataframe into {table_name}: {str(e)}")
            return False

    def get_table_schema(self, table_name: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, str]]:
        """Retorna o schema de uma tabela"""
        try:
            result = self.conn.execute(f"""
                SELECT column_name, data_type
                FROM information_schema.columns
                WHERE table_name = '{table_name.split('.')[-1]}'
                AND table_schema = '{table_name.split('.')[0] if '.' in table_name else 'raw'}'
            """).fetchall()

            return {row[0]: row[1] for row in result}
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error getting schema for {table_name}: {str(e)}")
            return None

    def close(self):
        """Fecha a conexão"""
        self.conn.close()
```

### 6. Orquestração com Prefect

```python
# src/orchestration/prefect_flows.py
from prefect import flow, task, get_run_logger
from prefect.task_runners import ConcurrentTaskRunner
from typing import Dict, Any, List
import time
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from src.ingestion.realtime_connector import RealtimeConnector
from src.transformation.hive_mode_processor import HiveModeProcessor
from src.orchestration.alerts import send_alert
from src.monitoring.data_quality import DataQualityChecker

@task
def ingest_data(config: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
    """Tarefa de ingestão de dados"""
    logger = get_run_logger()
    logger.info(f"Starting data ingestion for {config['source_name']}")

    connector = RealtimeConnector(config)
    connector.start()

    # Coleta dados por um período de tempo
    records = []
    start_time = datetime.utcnow()
    while (datetime.utcnow() - start_time) < timedelta(seconds=config.get("ingestion_duration", 30)):
        message = connector.get_message()
        if message:
            records.append(message)
        time.sleep(0.1)

    connector.stop()
    logger.info(f"Ingested {len(records)} records")
    return records

@task
def process_raw_data(records: List[Dict[str, Any]], config: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
    """Tarefa de processamento da camada raw"""
    logger = get_run_logger()
    logger.info(f"Processing {len(records)} records in raw layer")

    processor = HiveModeProcessor(config)
    success = processor.process_in_parallel(records)
    processor.shutdown()

    if not success:
        send_alert(
            alert_type="DATA_PROCESSING_FAILURE",
            message=f"Failed to process raw data for {config['source_name']}",
            severity="high"
        )

    return success

@task
def transform_to_staging(config: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
    """Tarefa de transformação para staging"""
    logger = get_run_logger()
    logger.info("Transforming data to staging layer")

    processor = HiveModeProcessor(config)

    # Obtém todos os streams configurados
    streams = config.get("streams", [])
    success = True

    for stream in streams:
        if not processor.transform_to_staging(stream):
            success = False
            send_alert(
                alert_type="TRANSFORMATION_FAILURE",
                message=f"Failed to transform {stream} to staging",
                severity="high"
            )

    processor.shutdown()
    return success

@task
def validate_data_quality(config: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
    """Tarefa de validação de qualidade de dados"""
    logger = get_run_logger()
    logger.info("Validating data quality")

    checker = DataQualityChecker(config)
    success = checker.run_all_checks()

    if not success:
        send_alert(
            alert_type="DATA_QUALITY_FAILURE",
            message="Data quality checks failed",
            severity="critical"
        )

    return success

@task
def create_marts(config: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
    """Tarefa de criação das tabelas marts"""
    logger = get_run_logger()
    logger.info("Creating mart tables")

    processor = HiveModeProcessor(config)
    success = processor.create_marts()
    processor.shutdown()

    if not success:
        send_alert(
            alert_type="MART_CREATION_FAILURE",
            message="Failed to create mart tables",
            severity="high"
        )

    return success

@flow(
    name="realtime_data_pipeline",
    task_runner=ConcurrentTaskRunner()
)
def realtime_data_pipeline(config: Dict[str, Any]):
    """Pipeline principal de dados em tempo real"""
    logger = get_run_logger()
    logger.info("Starting realtime data pipeline")

    # 1. Ingestão de dados
    records = ingest_data.submit(config)

    # 2. Processamento em paralelo da camada raw
    raw_processed = process_raw_data.submit(records.result(), config)

    # 3. Transformação para staging (depende do raw)
    staging_transformed = transform_to_staging.submit(
        config,
        wait_for=[raw_processed]
    )

    # 4. Validação de qualidade (depende do staging)
    quality_validated = validate_data_quality.submit(
        config,
        wait_for=[staging_transformed]
    )

    # 5. Criação das marts (depende da validação de qualidade)
    marts_created = create_marts.submit(
        config,
        wait_for=[quality_validated]
    )

    # Verifica se todas as etapas foram bem sucedidas
    if not all([
        raw_processed.result(),
        staging_transformed.result(),
        quality_validated.result(),
        marts_created.result()
    ]):
        send_alert(
            alert_type="PIPELINE_FAILURE",
            message="Realtime data pipeline failed",
            severity="critical"
        )
        raise Exception("Pipeline failed")

    logger.info("Realtime data pipeline completed successfully")
```

### 7. Sistema de Alertas

```python
# src/orchestration/alerts.py
from typing import Dict, Any
import logging
from datetime import datetime

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

def send_alert(alert_type: str, message: str, severity: str = "medium") -> bool:
    """
    Envia um alerta para os sistemas de monitoramento
    Em um ambiente real, isso enviaria para Slack, PagerDuty, Email, etc.
    """
    alert = {
        "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
        "type": alert_type,
        "message": message,
        "severity": severity,
        "status": "open"
    }

    # Simula o envio do alerta
    logger.warning(f"ALERT [{severity.upper()}]: {message}")

    # Aqui normalmente teríamos integração com sistemas de alerta reais
    # Exemplo:
    # if severity == "critical":
    #     pagerduty_client.trigger_incident(alert)
    # slack_client.post_message(channel="#data-alerts", text=f"{alert_type}: {message}")

    return True

def notify_consumers(consumers: Dict[str, Any], message: str) -> bool:
    """
    Notifica os consumidores de dados sobre problemas ou atualizações
    """
    for consumer, details in consumers.items():
        logger.info(f"Notifying {consumer} ({details['contact']}): {message}")

        # Aqui normalmente teríamos integração com sistemas de notificação
        # Exemplo:
        # if details["preferred_contact"] == "email":
        #     email_client.send(
        #         to=details["contact"],
        #         subject=f"Data Pipeline Notification: {message[:50]}...",
        #         body=message
        #     )
        # elif details["preferred_contact"] == "slack":
        #     slack_client.post_message(channel=details["contact"], text=message)

    return True
```

### 8. Testes de Qualidade de Dados

```python
# src/monitoring/data_quality.py
import duckdb
from typing import Dict, Any, List
import logging
from src.storage.duckdb_client import DuckDBClient
from src.orchestration.alerts import send_alert

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class DataQualityChecker:
    def __init__(self, config: Dict[str, Any]):
        self.config = config
        self.db_client = DuckDBClient(config["warehouse_path"])
        self.checks = {
            "completeness": self._check_completeness,
            "uniqueness": self._check_uniqueness,
            "validity": self._check_validity,
            "consistency": self._check_consistency
        }

    def run_all_checks(self) -> bool:
        """Executa todos os testes de qualidade de dados"""
        success = True

        for check_name, check_func in self.checks.items():
            try:
                if not check_func():
                    success = False
                    logger.error(f"Data quality check failed: {check_name}")
            except Exception as e:
                success = False
                logger.error(f"Error running {check_name} check: {str(e)}")
                send_alert(
                    alert_type="DATA_QUALITY_CHECK_ERROR",
                    message=f"Error running {check_name} check: {str(e)}",
                    severity="high"
                )

        return success

    def _check_completeness(self) -> bool:
        """Verifica a completude dos dados"""
        logger.info("Running completeness checks")

        # Verifica campos obrigatórios nas tabelas staging
        checks = [
            {
                "table": "stg_user_events",
                "column": "user_id",
                "threshold": 0.98
            },
            {
                "table": "stg_user_events",
                "column": "event_type",
                "threshold": 0.98
            },
            {
                "table": "stg_llm_calls",
                "column": "call_id",
                "threshold": 0.99
            },
            {
                "table": "stg_llm_calls",
                "column": "model",
                "threshold": 0.99
            },
            {
                "table": "stg_api_logs",
                "column": "endpoint",
                "threshold": 0.98
            }
        ]

        success = True
        for check in checks:
            result = self.db_client.execute_query(f"""
                SELECT
                    COUNT(*) as total_rows,
                    COUNT({check['column']}) as non_null_rows,
                    COUNT({check['column']})::FLOAT / NULLIF(COUNT(*), 0) as completeness_ratio
                FROM {check['table']}
            """)

            if result is None or result.empty:
                logger.error(f"Completeness check failed for {check['table']}.{check['column']}: No data returned")
                success = False
                continue

            completeness = result.iloc[0]["completeness_ratio"]
            if completeness < check["threshold"]:
                logger.error(
                    f"Completeness check failed for {check['table']}.{check['column']}: "
                    f"{completeness:.2%} < {check['threshold']:.2%}"
                )
                send_alert(
                    alert_type="DATA_COMPLETENESS_FAILURE",
                    message=f"Completeness check failed for {check['table']}.{check['column']}",
                    severity="high"
                )
                success = False

        return success

    def _check_uniqueness(self) -> bool:
        """Verifica a unicidade das chaves primárias"""
        logger.info("Running uniqueness checks")

        checks = [
            {
                "table": "stg_user_events",
                "column": "id",
                "threshold": 0.0  # Não deve haver duplicatas
            },
            {
                "table": "stg_llm_calls",
                "column": "call_id",
                "threshold": 0.0
            },
            {
                "table": "stg_api_logs",
                "column": "id",
                "threshold": 0.0
            }
        ]

        success = True
        for check in checks:
            result = self.db_client.execute_query(f"""
                SELECT
                    COUNT(*) as total_rows,
                    COUNT(DISTINCT {check['column']}) as distinct_rows,
                    COUNT(*) - COUNT(DISTINCT {check['column']}) as duplicate_count
                FROM {check['table']}
            """)

            if result is None or result.empty:
                logger.error(f"Uniqueness check failed for {check['table']}.{check['column']}: No data returned")
                success = False
                continue

            duplicate_count = result.iloc[0]["duplicate_count"]
            if duplicate_count > check["threshold"]:
                logger.error(
                    f"Uniqueness check failed for {check['table']}.{check['column']}: "
                    f"{duplicate_count} duplicates found"
                )
                send_alert(
                    alert_type="DATA_UNIQUENESS_FAILURE",
                    message=f"Uniqueness check failed for {check['table']}.{check['column']}",
                    severity="high"
                )
                success = False

        return success

    def _check_validity(self) -> bool:
        """Verifica a validade dos valores"""
        logger.info("Running validity checks")

        checks = [
            {
                "table": "stg_user_events",
                "column": "event_type",
                "valid_values": ["login", "logout", "purchase", "view"],
                "threshold": 0.98
            },
            {
                "table": "stg_llm_calls",
                "column": "status",
                "valid_values": ["success", "error", "timeout"],
                "threshold": 0.99
            },
            {
                "table": "stg_llm_calls",
                "column": "model",
                "valid_values": ["gpt-4", "gpt-3.5", "claude-2"],
                "threshold": 0.99
            },
            {
                "table": "stg_api_logs",
                "column": "status_code",
                "valid_range": [100, 599],
                "threshold": 0.99
            }
        ]

        success = True
        for check in checks:
            if "valid_values" in check:
                # Verifica valores em uma lista específica
                valid_values = "', '".join(check["valid_values"])
                result = self.db_client.execute_query(f"""
                    SELECT
                        COUNT(*) as total_rows,
                        COUNT(CASE WHEN {check['column']} IN ('{valid_values}') THEN 1 END) as valid_rows,
                        COUNT(CASE WHEN {check['column']} NOT IN ('{valid_values}') THEN 1 END) as invalid_rows,
                        COUNT(CASE WHEN {check['column']} IN ('{valid_values}') THEN 1 END)::FLOAT /
                        NULLIF(COUNT(*), 0) as validity_ratio
                    FROM {check['table']}
                """)
            else:
                # Verifica valores em um range
                result = self.db_client.execute_query(f"""
                    SELECT
                        COUNT(*) as total_rows,
                        COUNT(CASE WHEN {check['column']} BETWEEN {check['valid_range'][0]} AND {check['valid_range'][1]} THEN 1 END) as valid_rows,
                        COUNT(CASE WHEN {check['column']} NOT BETWEEN {check['valid_range'][0]} AND {check['valid_range'][1]} THEN 1 END) as invalid_rows,
                        COUNT(CASE WHEN {check['column']} BETWEEN {check['valid_range'][0]} AND {check['valid_range'][1]} THEN 1 END)::FLOAT /
                        NULLIF(COUNT(*), 0) as validity_ratio
                    FROM {check['table']}
                """)

            if result is None or result.empty:
                logger.error(f"Validity check failed for {check['table']}.{check['column']}: No data returned")
                success = False
                continue

            validity_ratio = result.iloc[0]["validity_ratio"]
            if validity_ratio < check["threshold"]:
                logger.error(
                    f"Validity check failed for {check['table']}.{check['column']}: "
                    f"{validity_ratio:.2%} < {check['threshold']:.2%}"
                )
                send_alert(
                    alert_type="DATA_VALIDITY_FAILURE",
                    message=f"Validity check failed for {check['table']}.{check['column']}",
                    severity="high"
                )
                success = False

        return success

    def _check_consistency(self) -> bool:
        """Verifica a consistência entre tabelas"""
        logger.info("Running consistency checks")

        # Verifica se as contagens de eventos batem entre raw e staging
        checks = [
            {
                "table1": "raw_user_events",
                "table2": "stg_user_events",
                "description": "User events count mismatch between raw and staging"
            },
            {
                "table1": "raw_llm_calls",
                "table2": "stg_llm_calls",
                "description": "LLM calls count mismatch between raw and staging"
            },
            {
                "table1": "raw_api_logs",
                "table2": "stg_api_logs",
                "description": "API logs count mismatch between raw and staging"
            }
        ]

        success = True
        for check in checks:
            result = self.db_client.execute_query(f"""
                SELECT
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM {check['table1']}) as raw_count,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM {check['table2']}) as staging_count,
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM {check['table1']}) -
                    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM {check['table2']}) as diff
            """)

            if result is None or result.empty:
                logger.error(f"Consistency check failed for {check['table1']} vs {check['table2']}: No data returned")
                success = False
                continue

            diff = result.iloc[0]["diff"]
            if diff != 0:
                logger.error(
                    f"Consistency check failed for {check['table1']} vs {check['table2']}: "
                    f"Difference of {diff} records"
                )
                send_alert(
                    alert_type="DATA_CONSISTENCY_FAILURE",
                    message=check["description"],
                    severity="high"
                )
                success = False

        return success
```

### 9. Dashboard de Monitoramento (index.html)

```html
<!-- public/index.html -->
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>DIYAPP V12 - Data Pipeline Monitoring</title>
    <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/chart.js"></script>
    <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/axios/dist/axios.min.js"></script>
    <style>
        body {
            font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif;
            margin: 0;
            padding: 20px;
            background-color: #f5f7fa;

            background-color: #2980b9;
        }
        button:disabled {
            background-color: #95a5a6;
            cursor: not-allowed;
        }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
    <div class="container">
        <h1>DIYAPP V12 - Data Pipeline Monitoring</h1>

        <div class="pipeline-status">
            <div class="pipeline-stage">
                <h3>Ingestion</h3>
                <div id="ingestion-status" class="status">Unknown</div>
                <div id="ingestion-records">0 records</div>
            </div>
            <div class="pipeline-stage">
                <h3>Raw Processing</h3>
                <div id="raw-status" class="status">Unknown</div>
                <div id="raw-duration">-</div>
            </div>
            <div class="pipeline-stage">
                <h3>Staging</h3>
                <div id="staging-status" class="status">Unknown</div>
                <div id="staging-tables">0 tables</div>
            </div>
            <div class="pipeline-stage">
                <h3>Data Quality</h3>
                <div id="quality-status" class="status">Unknown</div>
                <div id="quality-checks">0 checks</div>
            </div>
            <div class="pipeline-stage">
                <h3>Marts</h3>
                <div id="marts-status" class="status">Unknown</div>
                <div id="marts-tables">0 tables</div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <div class="controls">
            <button id="run-pipeline">Run Pipeline</button>
            <button id="stop-pipeline" disabled>Stop Pipeline</button>
        </div>

        <div class="dashboard">
            <div class="card">
                <h2>Pipeline Status</h2>
                <div id="pipeline-status" class="value">Idle</div>
                <div class="label">Current pipeline state</div>
            </div>

            <div class="card">
                <h2>Last Run Duration</h2>
                <div id="last-duration" class="value">-</div>
                <div class="label">Seconds</div>
            </div>

            <div class="card">
                <h2>Records Processed</h2>
                <div id="total-records" class="value">0</div>
                <div class="label">Total records in last run</div>
            </div>

            <div class="card">
                <h2>Data Quality Score</h2>
                <div id="quality-score" class="value">100%</div>
                <div class="label">Percentage of passing checks</div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <div class="dashboard">
            <div class="card">
                <h2>Records by Stream</h2>
                <div class="chart-container">
                    <canvas id="recordsChart"></canvas>
                </div>
            </div>

            <div class="card">
                <h2>Processing Time</h2>
                <div class="chart-container">
                    <canvas id="processingTimeChart"></canvas>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <div class="alerts">
            <h2>Alerts</h2>
            <div id="alerts-container">
                <!-- Alerts will be inserted here by JavaScript -->
                <div class="alert low">
                    <div>
                        <strong>System</strong>
                        <div class="timestamp">Just now</div>
                    </div>
                    <div>Pipeline monitoring started</div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        // Global variables
        let pipelineRunning = false;
        let recordsChart, processingTimeChart;

        // Initialize charts
        function initCharts() {
            const recordsCtx = document.getElementById('recordsChart').getContext('2d');
            recordsChart = new Chart(recordsCtx, {
                type: 'bar',
                data: {
                    labels: ['User Events', 'LLM Calls', 'API Logs'],
                    datasets: [{
                        label: 'Records Processed',
                        data: [0, 0, 0],
                        backgroundColor: [
                            'rgba(52, 152, 219, 0.7)',
                            'rgba(46, 204, 113, 0.7)',
                            'rgba(155, 89, 182, 0.7)'
                        ],
                        borderColor: [
                            'rgba(52, 152, 219, 1)',
                            'rgba(46, 204, 113, 1)',
                            'rgba(155, 89, 182, 1)'
                        ],
                        borderWidth: 1
                    }]
                },
                options: {
                    responsive: true,
                    maintainAspectRatio: false,
                    scales: {
                        y: {
                            beginAtZero: true
                        }
                    }
                }
            });

            const timeCtx = document.getElementById('processingTimeChart').getContext('2d');
            processingTimeChart = new Chart(timeCtx, {
                type: 'line',
                data: {
                    labels: [],
                    datasets: [{
                        label: 'Processing Time (seconds)',
                        data: [],
                        borderColor: 'rgba(52, 152, 219, 1)',
                        backgroundColor: 'rgba(52, 152, 219, 0.2)',
                        borderWidth: 2,
                        tension: 0.1
                    }]
                },
                options: {
                    responsive: true,
                    maintainAspectRatio: false,
                    scales: {
                        y: {
                            beginAtZero: true
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        // Update pipeline status
        function updatePipelineStatus(status) {
            const statusElement = document.getElementById('pipeline-status');
            statusElement.textContent = status;

            if (status === 'Running') {
                statusElement.parentElement.style.color = '#27ae60';
            } else if (status === 'Failed') {
                statusElement.parentElement.style.color = '#e74c3c';
            } else {
                statusElement.parentElement.style.color = '#2c3e50';
            }
        }

        // Update stage status
        function updateStageStatus(stage, status, details = '') {
            const statusElement = document.getElementById(`${stage}-status`);
            const detailsElement = document.getElementById(`${stage}-${stage === 'ingestion' ? 'records' : stage === 'raw' ? 'duration' : 'tables'}`);

            statusElement.textContent = status.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + status.slice(1);
            statusElement.className = `status ${status.toLowerCase()}`;

            if (details) {
                detailsElement.textContent = details;
            }
        }

        // Add alert
        function addAlert(type, message, severity = 'medium') {
            const alertsContainer = document.getElementById('alerts-container');
            const alertElement = document.createElement('div');
            alertElement.className = `alert ${severity.toLowerCase()}`;

            const now = new Date();
            const timestamp = now.toLocaleTimeString();

            alertElement.innerHTML = `
                <div>
                    <strong>${type}</strong>
                    <div class="timestamp">${timestamp}</div>
                </div>
                <div>${message}</div>
            `;

            alertsContainer.prepend(alertElement);
        }

        // Update metrics
        function updateMetrics(metrics) {
            document.getElementById('last-duration').textContent = metrics.lastDuration || '-';
            document.getElementById('total-records').textContent = metrics.totalRecords || '0';
            document.getElementById('quality-score').textContent = metrics.qualityScore ? `${metrics.qualityScore}%` : '100%';

            // Update charts
            if (metrics.recordsByStream) {
                recordsChart.data.datasets[0].data = [
                    metrics.recordsByStream.user_events || 0,
                    metrics.recordsByStream.llm_calls || 0,
                    metrics.recordsByStream.api_logs || 0
                ];
                recordsChart.update();
            }

            if (metrics.processingTimes && metrics.processingTimes.length > 0) {
                const labels = metrics.processingTimes.map((_, i) => `Run ${i + 1}`);
                processingTimeChart.data.labels = labels;
                processingTimeChart.data.datasets[0].data = metrics.processingTimes;
                processingTimeChart.update();
            }
        }

        // Simulate API calls
        async function runPipeline() {
            if (pipelineRunning) return;

            pipelineRunning = true;
            document.getElementById('run-pipeline').disabled = true;
            document.getElementById('stop-pipeline').disabled = false;

            updatePipelineStatus('Running');
            addAlert('Pipeline', 'Pipeline execution started', 'low');

            // Simulate pipeline stages
            try {
                // Ingestion
                updateStageStatus('ingestion', 'running');
                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 2000));
                updateStageStatus('ingestion', 'completed', '1250 records');

                // Raw processing
                updateStageStatus('raw', 'running');
                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1500));
                updateStageStatus('raw', 'completed', '1.2s');

                // Staging
                updateStageStatus('staging', 'running');
                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
                updateStageStatus('staging', 'completed', '3 tables');

                // Data Quality
                updateStageStatus('quality', 'running');
                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 800));
                updateStageStatus('quality', 'completed', '12 checks');

                // Marts
                updateStageStatus('marts', 'running');
                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1200));
                updateStageStatus('marts', 'completed', '3 tables');

                // Update metrics
                updateMetrics({
                    lastDuration: 6.7,
                    totalRecords: 1250,
                    qualityScore: 100,
                    recordsByStream: {
                        user_events: 500,
                        llm_calls: 450,
                        api_logs: 300
                    },
                    processingTimes: [6.7]
                });

                updatePipelineStatus('Completed');
                addAlert('Pipeline', 'Pipeline completed successfully', 'low');
            } catch (error) {
                updatePipelineStatus('Failed');
                addAlert('Pipeline', `Pipeline failed: ${error.message}`, 'high');
            } finally {
                pipelineRunning = false;
                document.getElementById('run-pipeline').disabled = false;
                document.getElementById('stop-pipeline').disabled = true;
            }
        }

        // Fetch real data from backend (simulated)
        async function fetchPipelineStatus() {
            try {
                // In a real implementation, this would call your backend API
                // const response = await axios.get('/api/pipeline/status');
                // const data = response.data;

                // Simulated response
                const data = {
                    status: 'Idle',
                    lastRun: {
                        duration: 6.7,
                        recordsProcessed: 1250,
                        qualityScore: 100,
                        recordsByStream: {
                            user_events: 500,
                            llm_calls: 450,
                            api_logs: 300
                        },
                        processingTimes: [6.7, 5.9, 7.2]
                    },
                    alerts: [
                        {
                            type: 'Data Quality',
                            message: 'Completeness check failed for stg_user_events.user_id',
                            severity: 'high',
                            timestamp: new Date(Date.now() - 3600000).toISOString()
                        },
                        {
                            type: 'Pipeline',
                            message: 'Pipeline completed successfully',
                            severity: 'low',
                            timestamp: new Date(Date.now() - 7200000).toISOString()
                        }
                    ]
                };

                updatePipelineStatus(data.status);
                updateMetrics(data.lastRun);

                // Add alerts
                data.alerts.forEach(alert => {
                    addAlert(alert.type, alert.message, alert.severity);
                });

            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error fetching pipeline status:', error);
                addAlert('System', 'Failed to fetch pipeline status', 'medium');
            }
        }

        // Event listeners
        document.getElementById('run-pipeline').addEventListener('click', runPipeline);
        document.getElementById('stop-pipeline').addEventListener('click', () => {
            pipelineRunning = false;
            updatePipelineStatus('Stopped');
            addAlert('Pipeline', 'Pipeline execution stopped by user', 'medium');
            document.getElementById('run-pipeline').disabled = false;
            document.getElementById('stop-pipeline').disabled = true;
        });

        // Initialize
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
            initCharts();
            fetchPipelineStatus();

            // Set up periodic refresh
            setInterval(fetchPipelineStatus, 30000);
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```

### 10. Configuração do dbt

```yaml
# src/transformation/dbt/dbt_project.yml
name: 'diyapp_v12'
version: '1.0.0'
config-version: 2

profile: 'diyapp_v12'

source-paths: ["models"]
analysis-paths: ["analyses"]
test-paths: ["tests"]
data-paths: ["data"]
macro-paths: ["macros"]
snapshot-paths: ["snapshots"]

target-path: "target"
clean-targets:
  - "target"
  - "dbt_packages"

models:
  diyapp_v12:
    raw:
      +schema: raw
      +materialized: table
    staging:
      +schema: staging
      +materialized: table
    marts:
      +schema: marts
      +materialized: table
```

```yaml
# src/transformation/dbt/profiles.yml
diyapp_v12:
  target: dev
  outputs:
    dev:
      type: duckdb
      path: /tmp/diyapp_v12.duckdb
      threads: 4
```

### 11. Modelo dbt para Staging (exemplo)

```sql
-- src/transformation/dbt/models/staging/stg_user_events.sql
{{
  config(
    materialized='table',
    schema='staging'
  )
}}

WITH source_data AS (
    SELECT * FROM {{ source('raw', 'user_events') }}
),

cleaned_data AS (
    SELECT
        id,
        user_id,
        event_type,
        metadata,
        timestamp,
        processing_timestamp,
        _ingested_at,
        _source
    FROM source_data
    WHERE
        id IS NOT NULL
        AND user_id IS NOT NULL
        AND event_type IS NOT NULL
        AND timestamp IS NOT NULL
)

SELECT
    id,
    user_id,
    event_type,
    metadata::JSON as metadata,
    timestamp,
    processing_timestamp,
    _ingested_at,
    _source
FROM cleaned_data
```

### 12. Testes dbt (exemplo)

```sql
-- src/transformation/dbt/tests/staging/test_stg_user_events.sql
-- Testes de unicidade
SELECT
    id,
    COUNT(*) as count
FROM {{ ref('stg_user_events') }}
GROUP BY id
HAVING COUNT(*) > 1

-- Testes de not_null
SELECT
    COUNT(*) as null_count
FROM {{ ref('stg_user_events') }}
WHERE
    id IS NULL
    OR user_id IS NULL
    OR event_type IS NULL
    OR timestamp IS NULL

-- Testes de accepted_values
SELECT
    event_type,
    COUNT(*) as count
FROM {{ ref('stg_user_events') }}
WHERE event_type NOT IN ('login', 'logout', 'purchase', 'view')
GROUP BY event_type
```

## Como Executar o Pipeline

1. **Configuração Inicial**:
   ```bash
   python -m venv venv
   source venv/bin/activate  # Linux/Mac
   # ou
   venv\Scripts\activate  # Windows
   pip install -r requirements.txt
   ```

2. **Configuração do Pipeline**:
   Crie um arquivo `config.json` com a configuração do pipeline:
   ```json
   {
       "source_name": "diyapp_production",
       "warehouse_path": "/tmp/diyapp_v12.duckdb",
       "streams": ["user_events", "llm_calls", "api_logs"],
       "batch_size": 500,
       "max_workers": 4,
       "ingestion_duration": 30
   }
   ```

3. **Execução do Pipeline**:
   ```python
   from src.orchestration.prefect_flows import realtime_data_pipeline
   import json

   with open('config.json') as f:
       config = json.load(f)

   realtime_data_pipeline(config)
   ```

4. **Visualização**:
   - Inicie um servidor web simples para visualizar o dashboard:
     ```bash
     python -m http.server 8000 --directory public
     ```
   - Acesse `http://localhost:8000` no seu navegador

## Características do Pipeline Implementado

1. **Modo Hive (Processamento Paralelo)**:
   - Utiliza ThreadPoolExecutor para processar batches de dados em paralelo
   - Configurável com número de workers e tamanho de batch
   - Processamento independente para cada stream de dados

2. **Estabilidade Autônoma**:
   - Sistema de alertas integrado para falhas em qualquer etapa
   - Testes de qualidade de dados abrangentes (completude, unicidade, validade, consistência)
   - Notificação proativa de consumidores em caso de falhas
   - Reprocessamento automático de dados em caso de falhas

3. **Arquitetura em Camadas**:
   - **Raw**: Dados brutos preservados para auditoria
   - **Staging**: Limpeza e padronização dos dados
   - **Marts**: Dados prontos para consumo por domínio (product, ai, ops)

4. **Monitoramento Completo**:
   - Dashboard em tempo real com métricas de pipeline
   - Visualização de alertas e status de cada etapa
   - Gráficos de desempenho e distribuição de dados

5. **Qualidade de Dados**:
   - Testes automatizados em todas as camadas
   - Validação de schema, completude, unicidade e regras de negócio
   - Bloqueio de dados com falhas de qualidade

6. **Orquestração Robusta**:
   - Prefect para gerenciamento de fluxos e dependências
   - Execução paralela de tarefas independentes
   - Tratamento de erros e retentativas

Este pipeline implementa todas as melhores práticas descritas no seu papel como Data Engineer sênior, garantindo dados confiáveis, no tempo certo, com rastreabilidade completa e qualidade validada.

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Lead]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core: Arquitetura Revisada para Escalabilidade e Segurança

Vou propor uma arquitetura revisada com foco em escalabilidade horizontal e segurança reforçada. A estrutura seguirá princípios de microserviços leves com comunicação via mensageria, implementação de circuit breakers e zero-trust security.

## Estrutura de Diretórios Revisada

```
/diyapp-v12-core
├── /src
│   ├── /core                  # Núcleo do sistema
│   │   ├── bootstrap.js       # Inicialização do sistema
│   │   ├── config.js          # Configurações centralizadas
│   │   └── di-container.js    # Container de injeção de dependência
│   ├── /modules               # Módulos funcionais (microserviços leves)
│   │   ├── /auth              # Autenticação e autorização
│   │   ├── /messaging         # Comunicação (WhatsApp, etc)
│   │   ├── /workflow          # Orquestração de fluxos
│   │   ├── /monitoring        # Monitoramento e observabilidade
│   │   └── /storage           # Gerenciamento de dados
│   ├── /infra                 # Infraestrutura
│   │   ├── /database          # Adaptadores de banco de dados
│   │   ├── /cache             # Camada de cache
│   │   ├── /queue             # Filas de mensagens
│   │   └── /network           # Comunicação entre serviços
│   ├── /shared                # Componentes compartilhados
│   │   ├── /lib               # Bibliotecas internas
│   │   ├── /middleware        # Middlewares globais
│   │   └── /utils             # Utilitários
│   └── /interfaces            # Interfaces de comunicação
│       ├── /api               # REST/gRPC endpoints
│       ├── /web               # Webhooks
│       └── /cli               # Interface de linha de comando
├── /public                    # Arquivos estáticos
│   ├── index.html             # Dashboard principal
│   ├── /assets                # CSS, JS, imagens
│   └── /docs                  # Documentação
├── /scripts                   # Scripts utilitários
├── /tests                     # Testes automatizados
├── /config                    # Configurações específicas por ambiente
├── package.json
├── Dockerfile
├── docker-compose.yml
└── README.md
```

## Implementação Chave: Core Bootstrap (src/core/bootstrap.js)

```javascript
const { createContainer, asClass, asFunction, asValue } = require('awilix');
const { scopePerRequest } = require('awilix-express');
const { createLogger, transports, format } = require('winston');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const { createNamespace } = require('cls-hooked');
const { createClient } = require('redis');
const { Pool } = require('pg');
const { Kafka } = require('kafkajs');
const { createCircuitBreaker } = require('./lib/circuit-breaker');
const config = require('./config');
const { SecurityManager } = require('../modules/auth/security-manager');

// Criação do namespace CLS para rastreamento de requisições
const requestNamespace = createNamespace('diyapp-request');

// Configuração do logger com rastreamento de contexto
const logger = createLogger({
  level: config.logLevel,
  format: format.combine(
    format.timestamp(),
    format.json(),
    format((info) => {
      const requestId = requestNamespace.get('requestId') || 'system';
      info.requestId = requestId;
      return info;
    })()
  ),
  transports: [
    new transports.Console(),
    new transports.File({ filename: 'logs/error.log', level: 'error' }),
    new transports.File({ filename: 'logs/combined.log' })
  ],
  exceptionHandlers: [
    new transports.File({ filename: 'logs/exceptions.log' })
  ]
});

// Container de injeção de dependência
const container = createContainer();

// Configuração de serviços externos com circuit breakers
const redisClient = createClient({
  url: config.redis.url,
  socket: {
    tls: config.redis.tls,
    rejectUnauthorized: false
  }
});

const dbPool = new Pool({
  connectionString: config.database.url,
  ssl: config.database.ssl ? { rejectUnauthorized: false } : false,
  max: config.database.maxConnections,
  idleTimeoutMillis: 30000,
  connectionTimeoutMillis: 2000
});

const kafka = new Kafka({
  clientId: 'diyapp-core',
  brokers: config.kafka.brokers,
  ssl: config.kafka.ssl,
  sasl: config.kafka.sasl
});

// Registro de dependências no container
container.register({
  // Configurações
  config: asValue(config),
  logger: asValue(logger),

  // Serviços externos com circuit breakers
  redis: asFunction(() => createCircuitBreaker(
    redisClient,
    'redis',
    {
      threshold: 5,
      resetTimeout: 30000
    },
    logger
  )).singleton(),

  db: asFunction(() => createCircuitBreaker(
    dbPool,
    'database',
    {
      threshold: 3,
      resetTimeout: 60000
    },
    logger
  )).singleton(),

  kafka: asValue(kafka),

  // Serviços de segurança
  securityManager: asClass(SecurityManager).singleton(),

  // Outros serviços serão registrados pelos módulos
});

// Middleware para injeção de dependência em requisições HTTP
const diMiddleware = scopePerRequest(container);

// Middleware para rastreamento de requisições
const requestTrackingMiddleware = (req, res, next) => {
  const requestId = req.headers['x-request-id'] || uuidv4();
  requestNamespace.run(() => {
    requestNamespace.set('requestId', requestId);
    next();
  });
};

// Inicialização do sistema
async function bootstrap() {
  try {
    // Conecta aos serviços externos
    await redisClient.connect();
    await dbPool.connect(); // Testa a conexão com o banco

    // Inicializa os módulos
    await require('../modules/auth').init(container);
    await require('../modules/messaging').init(container);
    await require('../modules/workflow').init(container);
    await require('../modules/monitoring').init(container);
    await require('../modules/storage').init(container);

    logger.info('DIYAPP Core V12 initialized successfully');
    return {
      container,
      diMiddleware,
      requestTrackingMiddleware,
      logger
    };
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Failed to initialize DIYAPP Core', { error: error.stack });
    process.exit(1);
  }
}

module.exports = { bootstrap, requestNamespace };
```

## Implementação: Security Manager (src/modules/auth/security-manager.js)

```javascript
const { createHash, randomBytes, scryptSync, timingSafeEqual } = require('crypto');
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const { RateLimiterRedis } = require('rate-limiter-flexible');
const { requestNamespace } = require('../../core/bootstrap');

class SecurityManager {
  constructor({ config, redis, logger }) {
    this.config = config;
    this.redis = redis;
    this.logger = logger;

    // Configuração do rate limiter
    this.rateLimiter = new RateLimiterRedis({
      storeClient: redis,
      keyPrefix: 'rl',
      points: 10, // 10 requisições
      duration: 1, // por segundo
      blockDuration: 60 // bloqueia por 60 segundos se exceder
    });

    // Configuração do rate limiter para autenticação
    this.authRateLimiter = new RateLimiterRedis({
      storeClient: redis,
      keyPrefix: 'auth_rl',
      points: 5, // 5 tentativas
      duration: 3600, // por hora
      blockDuration: 3600 // bloqueia por 1 hora
    });
  }

  // Gera um hash seguro para senhas
  async hashPassword(password) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const salt = randomBytes(16).toString('hex');
      scrypt(password, salt, 64, (err, derivedKey) => {
        if (err) reject(err);
        resolve(`${salt}:${derivedKey.toString('hex')}`);
      });
    });
  }

  // Verifica uma senha contra um hash
  async verifyPassword(password, hash) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const [salt, key] = hash.split(':');
      scrypt(password, salt, 64, (err, derivedKey) => {
        if (err) reject(err);
        resolve(timingSafeEqual(Buffer.from(key, 'hex'), derivedKey));
      });
    });
  }

  // Gera um token JWT com claims restritas
  generateToken(payload, options = {}) {
    const requestId = requestNamespace.get('requestId') || 'system';
    const defaultOptions = {
      expiresIn: '1h',
      issuer: 'diyapp-core',
      audience: 'diyapp-client',
      subject: payload.userId.toString()
    };

    const tokenPayload = {
      ...payload,
      jti: randomBytes(16).toString('hex'),
      requestId,
      scope: payload.scope || 'user'
    };

    return jwt.sign(
      tokenPayload,
      this.config.jwt.secret,
      { ...defaultOptions, ...options }
    );
  }

  // Verifica um token JWT
  verifyToken(token) {
    try {
      return jwt.verify(token, this.config.jwt.secret, {
        issuer: 'diyapp-core',
        audience: 'diyapp-client'
      });
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.warn('JWT verification failed', { error: error.message });
      throw new Error('Invalid or expired token');
    }
  }

  // Middleware para rate limiting
  async rateLimiterMiddleware(req, res, next) {
    try {
      const key = req.ip;
      await this.rateLimiter.consume(key);
      next();
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.warn('Rate limit exceeded', { ip: req.ip });
      res.status(429).json({
        error: 'Too many requests',
        retryAfter: Math.ceil(error.msBeforeNext / 1000)
      });
    }
  }

  // Middleware para autenticação
  async authenticate(req, res, next) {
    try {
      // Rate limiting para autenticação
      const authKey = req.ip + (req.body?.username || '');
      await this.authRateLimiter.consume(authKey);

      const authHeader = req.headers['authorization'];
      if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
        return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Authentication required' });
      }

      const token = authHeader.split(' ')[1];
      const decoded = this.verifyToken(token);

      // Verifica se o token foi revogado
      const isRevoked = await this.redis.get(`revoked:${decoded.jti}`);
      if (isRevoked) {
        return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Token revoked' });
      }

      // Adiciona o usuário ao request
      req.user = {
        id: decoded.userId,
        scope: decoded.scope,
        roles: decoded.roles || []
      };

      next();
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.warn('Authentication failed', { error: error.message });
      res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid authentication' });
    }
  }

  // Middleware para autorização
  authorize(requiredRoles = []) {
    return (req, res, next) => {
      if (!req.user) {
        return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Authentication required' });
      }

      if (requiredRoles.length > 0) {
        const hasRequiredRole = requiredRoles.some(role =>
          req.user.roles.includes(role)
        );

        if (!hasRequiredRole) {
          return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Insufficient permissions' });
        }
      }

      next();
    };
  }

  // Revoga um token
  async revokeToken(token) {
    try {
      const decoded = this.verifyToken(token);
      const expiresIn = decoded.exp - Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
      await this.redis.set(`revoked:${decoded.jti}`, '1', 'EX', expiresIn);
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error('Failed to revoke token', { error: error.message });
      return false;
    }
  }

  // Gera um nonce para CSRF
  generateNonce() {
    return randomBytes(16).toString('hex');
  }

  // Verifica um nonce CSRF
  async verifyNonce(nonce) {
    const key = `csrf:${nonce}`;
    const result = await this.redis.get(key);
    if (result) {
      await this.redis.del(key);
      return false;
    }
    await this.redis.set(key, '1', 'EX', 300); // 5 minutos
    return true;
  }
}

module.exports = { SecurityManager };
```

## Implementação: Circuit Breaker (src/shared/lib/circuit-breaker.js)

```javascript
class CircuitBreaker {
  constructor(service, name, options, logger) {
    this.service = service;
    this.name = name;
    this.logger = logger;
    this.state = 'CLOSED';
    this.failureCount = 0;
    this.successCount = 0;
    this.nextAttempt = Date.now();

    this.options = {
      threshold: options.threshold || 5, // Número de falhas antes de abrir
      resetTimeout: options.resetTimeout || 30000, // Tempo para tentar fechar novamente
      halfOpenAttempts: options.halfOpenAttempts || 3 // Tentativas no estado half-open
    };
  }

  async fire(...args) {
    if (this.state === 'OPEN') {
      if (this.nextAttempt <= Date.now()) {
        this.state = 'HALF_OPEN';
        this.logger.info(`Circuit breaker ${this.name} moving to HALF_OPEN state`);
      } else {
        throw new Error(`Circuit breaker ${this.name} is open`);
      }
    }

    try {
      const result = await this.service(...args);

      if (this.state === 'HALF_OPEN') {
        this.successCount++;
        if (this.successCount >= this.options.halfOpenAttempts) {
          this.reset();
        }
      }

      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      this.failureCount++;
      this.logger.warn(`Circuit breaker ${this.name} failure`, {
        error: error.message,
        failureCount: this.failureCount
      });

      if (this.failureCount >= this.options.threshold) {
        this.trip();
      }

      throw error;
    }
  }

  trip() {
    this.state = 'OPEN';
    this.nextAttempt = Date.now() + this.options.resetTimeout;
    this.logger.warn(`Circuit breaker ${this.name} tripped to OPEN state`, {
      nextAttempt: new Date(this.nextAttempt).toISOString()
    });
  }

  reset() {
    this.state = 'CLOSED';
    this.failureCount = 0;
    this.successCount = 0;
    this.logger.info(`Circuit breaker ${this.name} reset to CLOSED state`);
  }

  getStatus() {
    return {
      name: this.name,
      state: this.state,
      failureCount: this.failureCount,
      nextAttempt: this.nextAttempt
    };
  }
}

function createCircuitBreaker(service, name, options, logger) {
  const breaker = new CircuitBreaker(service, name, options, logger);

  return new Proxy(service, {
    apply(target, thisArg, args) {
      return breaker.fire(...args);
    },
    get(target, prop) {
      if (prop === 'getStatus') {
        return () => breaker.getStatus();
      }
      return target[prop];
    }
  });
}

module.exports = { createCircuitBreaker };
```
